<form><strong style="color:darkred; font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size:14pt">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第五十六</strong></form>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<a name="55p4473"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">攝決擇分中五識身相應地意地之六</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊善巧的決擇共分為三大科；第一大科總辨六相，以自性、義、差別、次第、攝、依止等六相來分別五蘊。第二大科廣顯別義，又以物類、極微、生起、安立、流轉、作業、剎那滅、獨非獨相、所行、相雜等十個角度說明五蘊。第三大科諸門決擇，又分為諸蘊相攝、諸蘊分位、諸蘊分別、和諸蘊建立四科。蘊善巧在本卷的範圍包括第二科的諸蘊分位、第三科的諸蘊分別，以及第四科諸蘊建立，蘊善巧的決擇到此結束，接著在本卷內廣分別界善巧、處善巧、及緣起善巧。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一卷從諸蘊分位開始，諸蘊分位是說二十四種心不相應行法，不相應行法與心不相應、與色不相應，而是依色、心的分位安立的假法，這在卷52已經研讀過了，不過卷52說到不相應行法是屬於假安立的諸法中，並沒有全部集中在一起說，現在卷56又再一次的決斷簡擇一番。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　蘊善巧的第三大科諸門決擇中第三科討論的是諸蘊分別，即是五蘊的分別，分成二部分說明，第一舉有色法為例，說到有色、有見、有對、有漏、有為、有諍、有愛味、依耽嗜、世間、墮界、過去、未來、現在、內、外、麤、細、劣、妙、遠、近、三界繫、三性、學、無學、非學非無學、見所斷、修所斷、無斷等，舉出很多例子詳細分別。第二例無色等，無色的四蘊也是一樣，有這些各別的情況。這些都是聖者對五蘊的微細觀察所顯。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科諸蘊建立，說明建立五蘊的道理，分建立蘊義、建立色義、建立名義、建立所攝、建立相應五科，將五蘊善巧的諸門決擇在此第四科處交待圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、諸蘊分位2　子一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科諸蘊分位，決擇諸蘊分位，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標示列舉出24個不相應行。在卷52已經詳細說過不相應行的內容，也可以再回去複習卷52的解釋，與《百法明門論》的解釋不同，本論有特別的解釋方法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：諸蘊分位有幾種？答：有多種。謂得、無想定等心不相應行，廣說如前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：諸蘊的分位有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有很多種，包括得、無想定等心不相應行，廣說如卷52中已經說過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》廣說如前者：如前決擇心不相應行法，一一差別應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#43887:40230">陵本五十二卷五頁4154</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　廣說如前，在本論卷52，1724~1738頁已決擇心不相應行法，應當了知不相應行法的一一差別相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、隨別釋20　丑一、得2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨別釋，接著各別解釋二十四個心不相應行法，分二十科；第一科得，說明得的建立與差別，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《百法直解》說：「得謂依一切法造作成就假立。」得，是成就不失義，得之一法，雖不是色法，也不是心法（心、心所），但也離不開色法、心法，單獨只有色法或心法，是不能建立的，故說：得之一法，乃是依心、心所、色三法假立之法。下面提出問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立得？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立得？得又有幾種？前面卷52，1730頁說得很詳細，這裡又將心不相應行法簡略地歸納說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明建立得的依止處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依因、自在、現行分位建立得。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依止種子為因，自在是指具足勢力，加上心心所法的現行，依此分位，而安立得。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4474"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明得的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂種子成就、自在成就、現行成就。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得，有成就不失的意思，又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、種子成就：約種子而言，種子未伏斷前，有能生果的潛能，是果現行增盛的遠因，名得；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、自在成就：約勢力而言，在引發於諸法的因緣中，未被其他因緣所阻礙，勢力具足，名得；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、現行成就：約現行而言，一切法自相現前，名得。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這三種成就在前面卷52，1731頁已經研讀過。其實得在部派佛教時，沒有安立種子，就安立得，為了解釋諸法成就不失的原因，他們所說的得是指新得，大乘所說得通於新舊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》依因自在現行分位等者：分位有三，一、因，二、自在，三、現行。依此分位，建立名得。由是說得略有三種，謂種子成就等。如前決擇中釋。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#43895:40441">陵本五十二卷九頁4174</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　得的分位有三種，一、因，二、自在，三、現行，依此分位，建立名得。故說得略有三種，包括種子成就、自在成就、現行成就，如前〈決擇分〉卷52，1731頁中已經解釋過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、無想定滅盡定及無想天2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無想定滅盡定及無想天，說明無想定、滅盡定及無想天的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立無想定、滅盡定及無想天？此三各有幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位建立無想定、滅盡定、及無想天？這三類各有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答3　卯一、無想定2　辰一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分三科；第一科無想定，先說無想定，又分二科；第一科明建立，說明無想定的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想定是二種無心定（無想定與滅盡定）之一。在《唯識心要》卷7說：沒有前六識，名無心。此時，因無前六識粗動心心所，令身平等和悅，如有心定（第六識與定心所相應，令心澄淨，稱有心定），也稱為定。說明無想定的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依已離遍淨貪，未離上貪，出離想作意為先名滅分位，建立無想定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：無想定已經降伏第三禪遍淨天的俱生貪，而證入第四禪，但尚未降伏第四禪的染心，認為諸想勞慮，令精神不能集中，諸想如病、如癰、如箭，於所生起種種想中，厭背而住，認為無想寂靜微妙，願意修習滅除一切心想的禪定，於是發起一種殊勝的期許與願望：「願我或一日乃至七日，或一劫，或一劫餘，能遮礙心心所，滅除一切心想！」由於厭背心想的作意，令心心所，由粗而細，由細而微，直到鄰次於定前的一剎那，微之又微的心，令前六識的心心所，暫時不起現行，依此前六識心心所滅的分位，建立無想定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣差別2　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明無想定的差別，分二科；第一科標，標出三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此無想定又有三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科自性，說明自性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性者，唯是善。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想定的自性是善，因為是由加行善心所引生的緣故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、補特伽羅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科補特伽羅，說明修無想定的人是凡夫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4475"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">補特伽羅者，在異生相續。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修無想定的人是誰？就是凡夫或外道等錯解涅槃的人；誤認無想天即是涅槃，有此非滅計滅的錯誤觀念。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科起，說明修無想定者將來到四禪天受異熟果</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">起者，先於此起，後於色界第四靜慮當受彼果。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　起者，先欲界修得此無想定，在欲界修無想定者，從欲界死歿後，受生於色界第四禪天中的無想天，享受無想天的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》自性唯是善者：謂依第四靜慮定地起故，定唯善故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想定依第四靜慮定地生起的，禪定一定是善的，故說無想定自性唯是善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、滅盡定2　辰一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科滅盡定，說明滅盡定的建立及差別，分二科；第一科明建立，說明滅盡定的建立。滅盡定與無想定，合稱二無心定，此二無心定，同樣是厭離心想的擾動，又同樣的具有定力能遮止轉識不生，由此建立二無心定。若只伏前六識心心所不起現行，名無想定；如果不但令前六識心心所不起現行，又更兼伏第七識俱生我執的心心所法，則稱滅盡定，唯第七識俱生法執與第八識仍在，不離根身，依此身心分位假立滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依已離無所有處貪，止息想作意為先名滅分位，建立滅盡定。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已遠離無所有處定的貪愛，已經不貪著無所有處定的三果或四果聖人，覺得念頭剎那生滅令人疲累，不想再這樣分別下去，因而作意停止前六轉識的受想心所，入於禪定，想要暫時停止心的分別，就在無所有處定中，作意止息受想心所，而入滅盡定；不但令前六識心心所不起現行，又兼伏第七識俱生我執及相應的心所，依此前六識心心所及第七識俱生我執及相應心所不活動的分位建立滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣差別2　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明滅盡定的差別，分二科；第一科標，標出三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　滅盡定也有三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科自性，說明滅盡定的自性是善</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性者，唯是善。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　滅盡定的自性也是善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、補特伽羅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科補特伽羅，入滅盡定的人包括證得八解脫的三果聖人，以及俱解脫阿羅漢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">補特伽羅者，在聖相續，通學無學。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　修滅盡定的人都是聖人，通於三果以上的有學聖者及無學的阿羅漢。但是能入滅盡定的三果聖者，必須已證得八解脫，無學阿羅漢是指俱解脫阿羅漢；不是所有的三果聖人及阿羅漢都能入滅盡定的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、起2　未一、託色依現前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科起，說明滅盡定的生起差別，分二科；第一科託色依現前，依聲聞乘及中觀學者說入滅盡定者先於欲界入，後於色界重現在前，託色所依才能現前故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4476"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">起者，先於此起，後於色界重現在前，託色所依方現前故。此據未建立阿賴耶識教。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　滅盡定生起，是指三果聖人先在欲界修得此定，壽盡生到色界天的五淨居天，之後在色界天上重新再入滅盡定。如果入滅盡定時前六轉識心心所不動，必須依託色法存在，才不會有斷滅論的危機，這是根據還沒有阿賴耶識教理的學者們所說。未建立阿賴耶識教，是指聲聞乘佛教及般若等教的學者們，認為入了滅盡定以後，前六轉識已滅沒有色身可以依止，若色身也沒有時，人就死掉了，這又不合道理。入滅盡定並沒有死，只是心心所暫時的休息，因此主張必須在欲界先起，後來在色界重現在前，才能夠入滅盡定。如果依止《解深密經》到了大乘唯識學，建立阿賴耶識教，生無色界的有情，也可以入滅盡定。由於有阿賴耶識在而不會斷滅。雖然無色界天有情沒有色身，因為有阿賴耶識在，即使入滅盡定，也沒有全部斷滅的危機。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、一切處現前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科一切處現前，若已建立阿賴耶識教，滅盡定則可於三界一切處現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若已建立，於一切處皆得現前。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果已經建立阿賴耶識教，在三界一切處都可以生起滅盡定。前面的說法是沒有建立阿賴耶識教之前，他們怕有斷滅的錯誤認知，所以說一定要在欲界先生起這個定，後來在色界再重修滅盡定，才可以證入。所以說一定要托色所依，才能夠修滅盡定。如果有阿賴耶識教，就沒有斷滅的問題，三界一切處都可以入滅盡定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於一切處皆得現前者：謂色無色界皆得現前故。由已建立阿賴耶識，略說諸法種子，一切皆依阿賴耶識故。義如因緣決擇中說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/51.htm#43924:40018">陵本五十一卷十九頁4133</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　於一切處皆得現前是指在色無色界都能入滅盡定，由於已經建立阿賴耶識，要略的說，一切諸法種子都依止在阿賴耶識中，在無色界也可以入滅盡定，因為無色有情的阿賴耶識並沒有滅除，出定以後這果報體還是可以生存的，義理如卷51，1714頁中建立阿賴耶識種子道理所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、無想天2　辰一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無想天，說明無想異熟的建立與差別，分二科；第一科明建立，依生無想天有情建立。外道修無想定，死後生無想天，成就所得的果報，稱為無想異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">依已生無想有情天中名滅分位，建立無想。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　已經生到無想天的有情，由於前六轉識心心所滅了，以此心心所滅的狀態，來建立無想異熟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣差別2　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，再詳細說明無想天有情的差別，分二科；第一科標，標出有三種差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此亦三種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想天有情的差別也有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋3　午一、自性</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科自性，說明無想天果報的自性為無覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">自性者，無覆無記。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想天的果報，異熟果報的阿賴耶識及種子自性都屬於無覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4477"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、補特伽羅</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科補特伽羅，生到無想天的人都是凡夫外道。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">補特伽羅者，唯異生性，彼非諸聖者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生到無想天的人都是凡夫或外道，不是聖人，聖人不會入這種定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午三、起</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科起，說明如何生無想天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">起者，謂能引發無想定思，能感彼異熟果；後想生已，是諸有情便從彼沒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無想果報的現起，是指生無想天的有情，因為執無想天為涅槃，依此出離想，引發入無想定的思願，作解脫入，在欲界修厭離想作意為先，就有這種異熟種子熏在阿賴耶識裡，命盡能夠感得無想天的果報。後生無想天有五百大劫的生命，出生後之前半劫有想；命終以前的半劫也有想，想現前的時候，這有情就從無想天死了。無想天的自性是無覆無記，和無想定的自性唯是善不一樣。無想定是屬於第四靜慮的定所生起的，定是善法，生於無想天，是依於阿賴耶識來說明，屬於無覆無記。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、命根2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科命根，說明命根的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生命的根本名命根，依《成唯識論》說，由前生善惡業力招感，令第八現行識具維繫執持色身不爛不壞的作用，稱為命根</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立命根？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立命根？命根又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明依業力所引果報住時決定分位建立命根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依業所引異熟住時決定分位，建立命根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依業力所引生的果報體，住世時間的多久，這樣的分位來建立命根。命根是一期的壽命，由過去生的業力決定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明命根的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂定不定故，愛非愛故，歲劫數等所安立故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　命根又有三種差別，包括決定、不決定；可愛、不非愛；命根長短的安立，或以年歲、或以劫數計算而安立的。定，是指有一定的壽命，如北俱盧洲人壽千歲，決定不會中夭。不定，是指壽量不決定，有中夭的情況，如南閻浮提人，壽量有短有長；西瞿陀尼人，壽命二百，也有夭逝；東毗提訶人，壽命三百，也有中夭。可愛的命根是指人天善趣眾生的命根。不可愛的命根是指三惡道眾生的命根。眾生的壽量多少？有的以年歲來計算，如欲界人天以年歲計算；有的以劫數來計算，如色、無色界天。三界眾生命根長短的安立各個不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4478"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》定不定故等者：除贍部洲人壽分量，所餘生處壽量決定。此贍部洲，或時壽命廣無有量，或時短促，壽量不定。由是當知定不定別。往五趣生，是名愛非愛別。有情壽量若少、若多，或以歲計，或以劫數計，如是名歲劫數等所安立。等言，等取有邊際、無邊際、自勢力轉、非自勢力轉差別應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除南贍部洲的人壽分量不一定，不一定會活到老年，中間有不平等的因緣出現也會中夭。其他洲的人壽量決定；《起世因本經》說，除北俱盧洲人壽決定，其餘三洲都有中夭。南贍部洲的人，有時壽命廣無有量，劫初時是無量壽，接下來是八萬四千歲；然後慢慢遞減，每一百年減一歲；減到三十、二十、最低十歲。佛在世時人壽平均八十歲，世人現在平均壽命應該是七十歲左右，但科技醫藥發達，也有說80幾歲。有些人胎死腹中，壽命極短，故說南贍部洲人壽量不定。在天、人、畜生、餓鬼、地獄五趣受生，名可愛與不可愛的差別；人天的命根是可愛的，三惡道的命根是不可愛的。有情的壽命是多少，有的是用年歲來算；有的是用劫數來計算。等字是指包括有邊際壽，如初果以上聖人，以及無邊際壽如凡夫，或由自己的力量可以延長如阿羅漢或菩薩等，或是不由自己的力量決定壽量長短，如一般凡夫。壽命也有很多差別相，在〈本地分‧有尋有伺地〉卷4中有詳細說明，這裡只是簡要的歸納。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、眾同分2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科眾同分，說明眾同分的建立與差別，眾是種類，同是相同，分是相似，種類相同相似，名眾同分，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立眾同分？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依據什麼分位來建立眾同分？眾同分又有幾種？此處眾同分是指有情而建立的；非情數就不討論它的眾同分了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明依諸有情相似分位安立眾同分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依諸有情相似分位，立眾同分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依止著各式各樣的有情相似的分位來安立眾同分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明眾同分的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。所謂種類同分、自性同分、工巧業處養命同分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眾同分又有三種，包括種類同分、自性同分、及工巧業處養命同分。《瑜伽論記》解釋種類同分是約種姓而言，如剎帝利，婆羅門、吠舍、首陀羅等；或約膚色而言，如黃種人、白種人、黑人等。自性同分是依種類同分，再細分下去，名自性同分。如以性別區分為男、女；以個性區分為溫柔或剛強，安立某種種姓者的特性等。工巧業處養命同分，以活命的方式來區分，如老師、醫生、木匠、工匠等差別，是以同一行業而為同分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》種類同分等者：界趣生類互相似性，是名種類同分。分位、體性、容色、形貌、音聲互相似性，是名自性同分。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在三界五趣中受生的有情種類，同界或同趣的有情互相有相似性，名為種類同分。比如同樣在欲界、同樣在色界、或同樣在無色界，同樣是人、是狗，或是鬼等，這是趣的同分。人天同屬於可愛的生類；地獄、餓鬼、畜生等，同屬於不可愛的生類。分位是指部分狀態相似名同分，如受用苦樂相同等；體性如自害、他害等；及容貌色相、外形相貌、說話聲音有互相相似性等，名為自性同分。還有工巧業處養命同分，這是以職業相同，或者是技能相同，說為同分，也就是工巧業處養命同分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、生2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科生，說明生的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。此等《成唯識論》卷二說：「本無今有，有位名生。」本來沒有這個法，借著種種條件的配合，因緣和合而有這個法顯現出來，在此法生出的時候，稱為生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立生？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依據什麼分位來建立生？生又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，先依現在分位建立生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4479"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依現在分位，建立生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依現在諸法能夠現前而建立生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明法生起的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。所謂剎那生、相續生、分位生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　法生起的差別又有三種，剎那生、相續生、分位生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 剎那生：一切有為法剎那剎那的新新生起，稱為剎那生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 相續生：從這一類有情壽盡之後，往生到另一類有情中去受生，生命相續，稱為相續生。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 分位生：包括增長生及心差別生；有情從嬰孩位，乃至往趣衰老位，稱為增長生。有情緣著不同的境界，有種種的心念生起來，有時心與樂受相應，有時與苦受相應，有時與不苦不樂受相應；有時有貪心，有時離貪心；廣說乃至或有善解脫心、或不善解脫心等，這些面對不同境界引生的心念差別，都稱為心差別生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》分位生者：謂即生差別中增長生、心差別生。義如前說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#43960:40308">陵本五十二卷六頁4161</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　分位生是指生差別中的增長生及心差別生，義理如前卷52，1726頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑六、老2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科老，說明老的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。《成唯識論》卷2說：在色心暫時相似相續，安住不變的階段，忽然起了前盛後衰的差別，而建立起異的名號，因此老又名異。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立老？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依據什麼分位來建立老？老又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，先依前後分位差別，建立老。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依前後分位，建立老。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依色心前後起了變化，稱為老。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明老的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂異性老、轉變老、受用老。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　老又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 異性老：色心前後性質不同，名異性老；如卷52，1728頁所說：「諸行剎那剎那轉名異性老」，由此能生身老、心老、壽老、變壞老、自體轉變老等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 轉變老：色心有種種的轉變，稱為轉變老；如卷52，1728頁所說，有情從善趣死後生到三惡道，五蘊自體完全轉變。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 受用老：諸根受用境界衰退名受用老，如前所說身老、心老、壽老、變壞老等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》受用老者：謂即老差別中身老、心老、壽老、變壞老。義如前說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#43967:40351">陵本五十二卷七頁4165</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　受用老是指種種的老差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 身老：如髮色衰變、皮膚緩皺、火力衰減、氣力損壞、性多疾病、黑黶間身、身脊傴曲、喘息奔急、形貌僂前、憑據杖策、昏昧羸劣、念慧衰退、諸根耄熟、功用破壞、諸行朽故、其形腐敗等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 心老：如樂受相應心變苦受相應心，善心變染污心，於可愛事中充滿希望變失望等；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 壽老：如時光迅速，每過一日，壽命就減少一日，乃至壽盡；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、 變壞老：如由富貴變成貧賤，健康變成有病，紅顏變醜顏，力壯變羸劣，充悅變沮喪等，義理如卷52，1728頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《增一阿含經》中有一個很小的故事。有一位長者年紀大了，病痛比較多，就去找佛陀，要求佛陀為他開示。佛陀告訴他說：人年老了本來就是會生病，生老病死苦是大家都難免的事情，但是修行人要修到身苦心不苦。身體雖然有苦受，但是心不要苦。佛陀只是簡單這樣跟他說，他聽不懂，又去問舍利弗，什麼是身苦心不苦？舍利弗尊者又為他解釋，所謂的身苦心不苦，是說身體是無常敗壞的，受想行識，也是一樣剎那無常敗壞，若不執著色受想行識是我、是我所，這樣心裡面就不會有痛苦了。地水火風依照法性的規則在成住壞空，無常敗壞，這件事情必須了解，是一個事實，若接受這種事實以後，不要將地水火風和合而成的色身，當作是我或我的身體，應該看成是地水火風暫時的因緣幻現，在無量劫的壽命裡面，只是暫時以這種方式呈現，時間到了當然要換成另外一個方式。就像雲要轉變成雨一樣，一定要轉變為另外一個方式而存在。如果心裡不執著色受想行識五蘊是我的話，心就不老了。這就是所謂身老心不老、身苦心不苦的定義。若要心不老不苦，要修無我觀，在五蘊裡面修無我觀。無我觀修成功了，心就不苦了。心雖不苦，身仍還是會苦，由於以前所造作的業力，使色身會有老病死的現象，老病死是一個自然的理則。這身體會生病很正常；但是心裡不能生病，任何人若不執著身體是我的話，苦則會減少很多。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑七、住2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科住，說明住的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。《成唯識論》卷2說：「生位暫停，即說為住。」色心諸法生起之後，暫時安住，稱為住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4480"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立住？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依據什麼分位來建立住？住又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明依諸行生時建立住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：即依生分位，建立住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依色心諸行剎那生時，暫時安住的分位來建立住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明住的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂剎那住、相續住、立制住。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　住又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 剎那住：已生色心諸行剎那安住名剎那住；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 相續住：有情已生五蘊，由食為依相續現前，器世間在壞、空劫之前相續安住，稱為相續住；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 立制住：又名立軌範住，如不同國家地區各有管理制度，使人民安居樂業，這些為人民或家庭制定的法律、憲法、法規等名立制住。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》立制住者：此即住差別中立軌範住。義如前說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#43975:40381">陵本五十二卷八頁4168</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　立制住就是住差別中的立軌範住，義理如前卷52，1728頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑八、無常2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科無常，說明無常的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。《百法直解》說：無常，也稱作滅，借著色心諸法，由於因緣分散，色心諸法從暫有的階段，還歸於虛無的狀態，假名為無常。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立無常？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依據什麼分位來建立無常？無常又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明無常的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依生已壞滅分位，建立無常。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：諸法出生以後又壞滅，從有而無，依此壞滅分位建立無常。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細說明無常的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4481"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂壞滅無常、轉變無常、別離無常。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無常又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 壞滅無常：在〈本地分‧聲聞地〉卷34無常十行中已經有說過。若一切有為諸行才生即滅，名壞滅無常；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 轉變無常：是卷34所說的變異無常，內事有十五種變異，與八種變異因緣，外事有十六種變異。若可愛諸行轉成不可愛，名轉變無常；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 別離無常：若財物散失，名位遠離，或是眷屬分散等，名別離無常。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》壞滅無常等者：聲聞地說：由變異行、滅壞行，及別離行觀無常性。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/34.htm#43984:27478">陵本三十四卷三頁2739</a>）此說三種，隨應當知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈本地分‧聲聞地〉說：由變異行、滅壞行，及別離行觀無常性。此處說三種，對照卷34，1100頁所說，隨其所相應的即可了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑九、名句文身2　寅一、舉名身2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科名句文身，說明名句文身的建立與差別，名，是名字、名詞或名稱之意。身，是聚集之意，單一名稱為名，二種名以上聯合，稱為名身。句，就是句子，身是集合之義，一句是句，二句以上，方稱句身。文，就是字，為名句之所依。文，具有能彰顯之義，或顯名、句，或顯義理。一字為文，二字以上稱為文身，分二科；第一科舉名身，先舉出名身，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立名身？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立名身？名身又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明名身的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依假言說分位，建立名身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依假安立的言說來建立名身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，詳細的說明名身的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂假設名身、實物名身、世所共了不了名身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名身又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、假設名身：〈攝釋分〉卷81，2445頁說：於內身假名安立我及有情；於外色聲香味觸法，安立這是瓶子，那是衣服等。於諸法和合相，假名安立各種名稱。名所依的義，並沒有真實的法體，這是假設名身。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、實物名身：於因緣所生的依他起法，如眼耳鼻舌身，色聲香味觸法等諸根境界當中，安立眼耳鼻舌身，或色聲香味觸等，這是實物名身。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、世所共了、不了名身：前二種名身為世間人所共同了解、認可的，稱為世所共了名身。世間人所不了解、不明白的，稱為世所不了名身。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈攝釋分〉卷81，2445頁提出十二種的名身。這裡列舉出其中的四種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、例句身等2　卯一、例同</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例句身等，以名身為例，推理句身等道理，分二科；第一科例同，說明如名身，句身、文身等道理也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如名身，句身、文身，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如名身是這樣子，句身及文身也一樣有四種。假設句身、實物句身，還有世所共了、不了句身；文身也一樣，有假設文身、實物文身、世所共了、不了文身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、顯別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯別，顯示它的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中差別者，謂標句、釋句、音所攝、字所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　但其中也有差別，句身有標句、釋句，標出法的特性名標句，如說善性、惡性等；解釋法的特性稱為釋句，如說正趣善士，或說這是好人，因為他心裡有很多善良的思想等。《百法明門論》說：名、句、文三者都依色、聲、法塵分位假立。此處說文身也有音韻所攝及字所攝的差別；音韻所攝是指語言中所有名、句及文字，依聲假立，可以發出有韻調的聲音，稱為音韻所攝。國語注音符號中有ㄅㄆㄇㄈㄉㄊㄋㄌㄍㄎㄏㄐㄑㄒㄓㄔㄕㄖㄗㄘㄙ，是聲母；ㄧㄨㄩ是介母；ㄚㄛㄜㄝㄞㄟㄠㄡㄢㄣㄤㄥㄦ，是韻母，由聲母加介母或韻母合起來，就能發出聲音。字所攝是指若書冊中所有名、句及文字，依色立，稱為字所攝；音所攝的是聲塵；字所攝屬於色塵，就是所謂的文身。此外若心想中所有名、句及文字，依法立，即是法塵。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　名、句、文都是依色、聲、法三塵而假立的，別無自體。這是以娑婆世界眾生，眼、耳、意三種根識特別明利，故偏依三塵安立名句文。若以他方世界眾生，餘根識利，則香飯、天衣等，都可依之假立名句文。如眼根利者，依光明立名句文；鼻根利者，依妙香立名句文；舌根利者，依妙味立名句文；身根利者，依觸塵立名句文；意根利者，則依法塵立名句文。統論十方佛土，六塵都可假立名句文，六塵都是佛之言教，也是修行的法門，也是甚深微妙之教理，只要能顯示義理，一切諸法，都可為如來言教之體性，或揚眉瞬目，或拈花微笑，或蹙眉呻吟、咳嗽幾聲、或憶念、或動搖&hellip;&hellip;等表顯於法，總之不一定由言說或文字而有諸法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4482"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》音所攝字所攝者：此說名身文身差別應知。由依止名、或唯依文了達音韻，是故說彼名音所攝。由名身、句身所依止字，是謂文身，是故說文名字所攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，音所攝、字所攝，是指名身文身的差別。《披尋記》這樣解釋。不過其他的地方，也有不一樣的解釋。由依止名身，或依止字，可以了達音韻。其實句子也可以了達它的音韻，就是音所攝。由名身、句身所依止的字，就是文身，故說文是字所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十、異生性2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科異生性，說明異生性的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。故《華嚴經探玄記》說：「異生者，執異見而生，故曰異生，即舊名凡夫也。」《成唯識論》卷一說異生性之建立，約眾生尚未見道之前，未永斷三界見惑煩惱種子，未成就諸無漏聖法，假立異生性之名。因此，異生之性，是指三界見所斷的種子，依此種子，令眾生起異類見、造異類業、受異類果，所以稱作異生性。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立異生性？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立異生性？異生性又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明異生性的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依未生起一切出世聖法分位，建立異生性。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依止還沒證得我法二空真如，尚未成就一切出世間聖人之法的分位，來建立異生性。《大乘百法明門論開宗義記》說：「諸聖者，皆名同生；而諸凡愚，名曰異生。」此意即謂：一切聖人，同見到真空之理，不起我見，故名同生；而諸凡夫，愚癡闇冥，沒有智慧，由於有我見，而生起各種不同的見解，故名異生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明異生性的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂欲界繫、色界繫、無色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　異生性又有三種：為欲界煩惱所繫縛的欲界凡夫，為色界煩惱所繫縛的色界凡夫；還有為無色界煩惱所繫縛的無色界凡夫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十一、流轉2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科流轉，說明流轉的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。本論卷52說：「諸行因果相續不斷性，是謂流轉。」流是相續之義，轉是生起之義，流轉，就是相續生起之義。所指即是有為法之因果，一切有為法，由因感果，果續於因，因果相續，前後不停，名流轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立流轉？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立流轉？流轉又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明流轉的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依因果相續分位，建立流轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依因果不斷相續的分位來建立流轉。《成唯識論》卷3說明本宗的因果義，指出因果相續不斷，總不離現前一剎那法。觀現在法有引後法的作用，假說現在法為後果之因；又觀現在法有酬前因相，假說現在法為前因之果，所以將現前一剎那法，說成因果相續不斷，前因位滅，後果即生，如稱兩頭，低昂時等，如是因果相續如流，稱為流轉。總之，因果體性不同，生滅事異，都是識所變現，同在一時，更非前後，如是因果，剎那生滅，相續不斷，謂之流轉。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4483"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明流轉的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂剎那展轉流轉、生展轉流轉、染汙清淨展轉流轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　流轉又有三種差別：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、剎那展轉流轉：心念剎那生滅，非常非斷，名剎那展轉流轉；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、生展轉流轉：凡夫的生命體在三界中往返不停，名生展轉流轉；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、染汙清淨展轉流轉：凡夫有時染污心生，有時清淨心生，三性心生相續不絕，名染汙清淨展轉流轉。約十二緣起而言，由無明故有行，乃至由生故有老死，此生故彼生，名順流流轉，屬染汙展轉流轉一類；若就聖人所修道品，無明滅故行滅，乃至生滅故老死滅，此滅故彼滅，名逆流流轉，屬清淨展轉流轉一類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》染汙清淨展轉流轉者：如前說有順流流轉，謂順緣起。又有逆流流轉，謂逆緣起。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#44011:40612">陵本五十二卷十三頁4189</a>）此說染汙清淨，如次應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文所說有順流流轉，指順緣起；無明緣行，行緣識，乃至生緣老死，純大苦聚；又有逆流流轉，指逆緣起；無明滅故行滅，乃至生滅故老死滅。此處說染汙清淨，如其次第指染淨二種緣起應當了知。如卷52，1736頁所說。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十二、定異2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科定異，說明定異的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。定，是決定，異，是不同，指善因樂果，惡因苦果。各有因果，涇渭分明，決定不相混淆，不論如來出世，或不出世，因果法則，本來是如此。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立定異？此復幾種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立定異？定異又有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明定異的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依法別相分位，建立定異。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依法和法之間有各別的相狀，決定有差別，沒有雜亂性的分位來建立定異。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明定異的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂相定異、因定異、果定異。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　定異又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相定異：因果體相決定不同，善因樂果，惡因苦果，各有因果，體性相狀不同；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、因定異：善惡業因決定不同，善因感人天樂果，惡因感三惡趣苦果；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、果定異：苦樂果報決定不同，苦果苦受相應，樂果樂受相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂相定異等者：如前說有流轉、還滅定異，一切法定異，領受定異，住定異。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#44018:40624">陵本五十二卷十三頁4190</a>）如是一切，名相定異。即彼諸法若因、若果，決定差別無雜亂性，名因定異、果定異。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如卷52，1736頁所說的相定異，屬於相狀上決定的差別性，如流轉、還滅、十二處、領受、住時、形量等諸有為法的差別，這一切都名為相定異。由於因不同，決定得到不同的果。這些差別決定不會夾雜混亂，這就是因定異及果定異。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、流轉、還滅定異：流轉指四諦中之苦諦與集諦，是生死流轉之因果；還滅是四諦中之滅諦與道諦，是涅槃還滅之因果，流轉還滅二門決定不同。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、一切法定異：一切法十二處攝盡，十二處各各決定不同。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、領受定異：一切受不出苦、樂、捨三受，三受各各決定不同。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、住定異：有情及器世間暫時安住之壽量或期限各各決定不同。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、形量定異：欲界有情及色界有情，所受生之身形大小，各各決定不同；外分四大洲等形量，也是各各決定不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十三、相應2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科相應，說明相應的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。因果相稱名相應；前面針對因果之相續性假立流轉之法；針對因果之別異性而假立定異之法；此處針對因果之相稱性而假立相應之法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4484"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立相應？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：以什麼分位來建立相應？相應有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明相應的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依因果相稱分位，建立相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依因和果是相稱的分位，建立相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明相應的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂和合相應、方便相應、稱可道理所作相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　相應又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、和合相應：《瑜伽論記》說：「善感於樂；惡招於苦」，善因招感樂果，比如修五戒十善可以感得人天樂果；惡因招感苦果，比如造上中下品十惡業將感得三惡道的苦果，這是和合相應；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、方便相應：《瑜伽論記》說：加行智相對於根本智來說，就是方便相應，還不是究竟相應，比如誦經、拜佛、修四念處未成就前都屬於方便相應；於緣起諸法，能安立相稱言說，建立正確因緣，開顯世出世法的因果道理，稱為方便相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、稱可道理所作相應：智慧與觀待、作用、證成、法爾四種道理相應，簡說就是智慧和真理相應，名為稱可道理所作相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》和合相應等者：極微已上，一切有方分色更互和合，是名和合相應。如集論說。（三卷九頁）彼彼諸法為等言說、為等建立、為等開解諸勝方便，是名方便相應。與四道理相應，謂觀待道理等，是名稱可道理所作相應。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《集論》卷3說：極微已上，這一些佔有空間的色法，互相和合，就是和合相應。於各式各樣的緣起諸法，能正確記別，使能詮的言說相稱於所詮的諸法，如說五蘊、十二處等；能正確建立諸法的因緣，如由惑業苦而有生死輪迴；能正確開示世出世法的因果道理，如苦集滅道等四諦道理，稱為方便相應；與四種道理：觀待道理、作用道理、證成道理、法爾道理相應，是名稱可道理所作相應。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十四、勢速2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科勢速，說明勢速的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。勢速是變化或動作迅速，《百法直解》說：「依於色心諸法遷流，不暫停住假立。」不論色法、心法，都像江河中的流水一般，迅速的向前奔流。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立勢速？此復幾種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立勢速？勢速有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明勢速的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4485"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依迅疾流轉分位，建立勢速。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依色心諸法迅速地流動轉變的分位來建立勢速。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明勢速的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂諸行勢速、士用勢速、神通勢速。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　勢速又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、諸行勢速：諸行就是一切有為法，經中說，一彈指頃有六百個生滅，有為法的剎那生滅是很快速的；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、士用勢速：指人、象、馬、飛禽走獸，走動或飛行的速度非常地快速，或藥叉、天人，他們的速度更快。士用就是人、有情的意思。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、神通勢速：神通的速度當然很快，經典裡面說屈伸臂頃就到色究竟天等，這是屬於神通的速度，也是很快速。</span></span></span></div>
