<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》士用勢速等者：如前說：有地行有情輕健勢速，謂人、象、馬等。或有空行有情勢速，謂諸飛禽、空行藥叉及諸天等。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#44035:40656">陵本五十二卷十四頁4192</a>）此攝彼二應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前文說：有一類在地上居住的有情，他們身形輕便，健朗行走的速度很快，比如說人、象、馬等，這些稱為地行有情；或有一類空行的有情也是速度很快，如飛禽、空行藥叉、及諸天等。如卷52，1737頁所說，此處勢速包括地行及空行有情二種應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十五、次第2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科次第，說明次第的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。次第是順序，譬如尊卑上下，各守法則，循序漸進，前後不亂，名為次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立次第？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立次第？次第有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明次第的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依一一行流轉分位，建立次第。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依諸有為法流轉的分位，無明緣行，乃至生緣老死，來建立次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，說次第的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂剎那流轉次第、內身流轉次第、成立所作流轉次第。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　次第又有三種，依《瑜伽論記》的解釋：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、剎那流轉次第：也就是諸行流轉的次第，指諸行前後念念相續流轉的次第；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、內身流轉次第：指在家及出家行住次第，卷52說：在家行住次第；早上起床，刷牙洗臉，穿戴整齊，上班工作，沐浴打扮，吃飯睡覺等；出家行住次第如整理衣服，入聚落乞食，巡次而行，受如法食，還出安坐，吃完洗手，盪缽洗腳，入空閒室，讀誦經典，如理思惟。日間宴坐經行，淨修其心，斷滅諸障，晚上9點到隔日早上3點寢息，3點起床到6點繼續宴坐經行，淨修其心，6點之後又開始新的一日；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、成立所作流轉次第：指劫初外器世間界之前後安布的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4486"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》內身流轉次第等者：如前說：有流轉次第，謂無明緣行，廣說乃至生緣老死。又說：或有在家、出家行住次第。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#44043:40681">陵本五十二卷十四頁4194</a>）此中二種，如次應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前卷52，1737頁說：有流轉次第，指無明緣行，廣說乃至生緣老死。又說：或有在家、出家日常生活行住坐臥次第。此中無明緣行，廣說乃至生緣老死，是指內身流轉次第，在家及出家行住次第名成立所作流轉次第，此中二種次第，如其次第應當了知。韓居士此解與《瑜伽論記》解釋不同。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十六、時2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科時，說明時的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。時是時間，《雜集論》卷2說：時是指於因果相續流轉，假立為時。何以故？由有因果相續轉故。若此因果，已生已滅，立過去時；此若未生，立未來時；已生未滅，立現在時。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立時？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立時？時有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明時間的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依行相續不斷分位，建立時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依有為法相續不斷的分位，來建立時間的觀念，故時間也是假法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明時間的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂去、來、今。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　時間有三種；過去、未來，及現在。時間是假法，長短不定故；如說一晝夜，在人間為二十四小時，而四王天一晝夜，是人間五十年，忉利天一晝夜，則是人間一百年，同是一晝夜，卻長短不定，故說時間為假立之法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十七、方2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科方，說明方的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。方是方位，指色法存在於空間的方向與位置。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立方？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立方？方有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明方的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依所攝受諸色分位，建立方。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依所攝受的內外色法前後左右的分位來建立方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛說明方的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4487"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂上、下、傍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　方又有三種；上方、下方、或者是傍邊。其實還有很多，但是簡單歸納成三種。傍就是包括東西、東南、東北、西南、西北及左右等。一般說方位有四方，如東、西、南、北；八方，就是四方加上東南、西南、西北、東北；十六方，即八方的中間，再加上東北東、北北東、東南東、南南東、西北西、北北西、西南西、南南西等八個方位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十八、數2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十八科數，說明數的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。數就是數字，一種度量諸法大小多寡的名稱。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立數？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立數？數有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明數的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依法齊量表了分位，建立數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：齊就是同等的意思，也就是等於。諸法等於多少數量，為了表示諸法數量的多少，依這樣的分位建立數目字；比如說諸法等於0，或者等於1，或者等於2。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明數的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂一數、二數、多數。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　數的差別有三種，有一個數名為單數，二個數名為雙數，或者是多數，又名複數。蕅益大師《百法直解》說：「數者，依於諸法多少相仍相待假立。」數字的建立，是依著有為諸法彼此之間相待關係而安立的，於是才有一十百千乃至阿僧祇等數字的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相仍的仍字，當因循或沿襲說；即後一個數字是因循著前一個數字而來，如《三字經》說：「一而十，十而百，百而千，千而萬」。又根據《三藏法數》的記載，數法有三等，即下等、中等及上等，由此三等數法，也可看出前後二個數字間相仍的情形，即：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「下等數法」十十增變：十是重複十個一而成，所謂一十為十。百是重複十個十而成，所謂十十為百。千是重複十個百而成，所謂十百為千。萬是重複十個千而成，所謂十千為萬。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「中等數法」百百增變：如一百洛叉（十萬為洛叉）為一俱胝（千萬為俱胝）等。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　「上等數法」倍倍增變：如俱胝俱胝為一阿庾多等。又印度有十大數，皆屬上等數法，即阿僧祇、無量、無邊、無等、不可數、不可稱、不可思、不可量、不可說、不可說不可說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、相待，即互相對待，數字概念的形成，乃起源於相待。張三比李四高一點；今天比昨天熱；從台北到埔里，比台北到新竹遠；做一件僧服要多少布，才不至於過多或過少等，總之在日常生活中，由於諸法的長短、大小、多寡、高低等相對待的結果，就假立出數字來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑十九、和合2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十九科和合，說明和合的建立與差別，分二科；第一科問，提問。諸法很和諧地聚會融合為一稱為和合。卷52說：「云何和合？謂能生彼彼諸法、諸因、諸緣，總略為一，說名和合。」如眼識九緣生，九緣是指 1、眼根 2、色境 3、作意 4、空 5、明 6、眼識種子 7、分別依 8、染淨依 9、根本依，以上九緣，互相鄰助，俱時合力，不相乖違，眼識才能生起，眼識與根等九緣，稱為和合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立和合？此復幾種？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立和合？和合有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明建立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明建立，說明和合的建立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：依所作支無闕分位，建立和合。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：依所作事的因緣沒有缺少的分位建立和合。一切法由緣而起，因緣具足諸法就現前，根身器世間諸法都是由因緣和合而生。追求菩提大道的行者，要修六度萬行，待六度圓滿，因緣具足就能成就無上正等正覺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、廣差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣差別，廣泛的說明和合的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此復三種。謂集會和合、一義和合、圓滿和合。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　和合又有三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 集會和合：大眾聚集在一起，比如說，我們在這裡上課，研讀本論，就稱為集會和合，集會和合就是聚會；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 一義和合：一義就是一個境界，諸心心所同所緣一個境界。例如大家都在研讀本論，這個也可以稱為一義和合，依同一個所緣境來作事情，就是一義和合；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 圓滿和合：這件事圓滿了，比如說，蓋房子，房子蓋好了，得到究竟時，就是圓滿和合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4488"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》集會和合等者：如前說：有清淨和合，謂十二種無雜集會，即自他圓滿等。又有世俗和合，謂諸有情依等意樂增上力故，互不相違，無諍無訟，亦不乖離。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/52.htm#44071:40543">陵本五十二卷十二頁4183</a>）即此集會和合、圓滿和合應知。又復前說有領受和合等，即此一義和合，謂於一所作事更互相應故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前卷52，1734頁說，有清淨和合，指十二種無雜集會，即自他圓滿等；清淨是指涅槃，成就涅槃需要十種因緣和合，即自他各五法，合十種圓滿；又有世俗和合，指世間的和合，要依相等的意樂，互相增上的力量，大家在一起，不做互相違背的事，沒有諍論訴訟，也不互相背叛遠離，才能圓滿成辦所作事業。這是卷52所說，就是這裡的集會和合及圓滿和合，應當了知。又前卷52說有領受和合等，就是這裡所說的一義和合，一義就是一件事情，或者一個境界，同一個境界大家互相相應，就是一義和合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二十、不和合</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十科不和合，說明不和合的建立與差別。諸法之間，彼此互相妨礙、對立，稱為不和合，如水與火，冰與炭，正與邪，霜雹與稻麥，都是不和合之例。或眼識九緣生中，任缺一緣，則眼識之生緣不和合；或十二因緣中，隨缺一支，則有情生死之因緣不和合。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：依何分位建立不和合？此復幾種？答：與和合相違，應知不和合若分位、若差別。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依什麼分位來建立不和合？不和合有幾種？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：與前面的和合相反的情況就是不和合，約所作支有闕的分位建立不和合；不和合有三種；集會不和合、一義不和合、圓滿不和合。在家人若和合則家和萬事興，不和合則家破人散；出家人若和合共住，能住持佛法、令正法久住，若不和合，則破壞佛教，令正法隱沒，邪法熾盛。　</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、諸蘊分別2　子一、辨2　丑一、舉有色等29　寅一、有色</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科諸蘊分別，分二科；第一科辨，辨明諸蘊所攝義及所攝種類，又分二科；第一科舉有色等，先舉出有色的定義及有色法的種類，分成二十九科，用二十九種不同的角度來討論色蘊，包括有色、有見、有對、有漏、有為、有諍、有愛味、依耽嗜、世間、墮界、過去、未來、現在、內、外、麤、細、劣、妙、遠、近、三界繫、三性、學、無學、非學非無學、見所斷、修所斷、無斷，用這麼多種的角度來討論色蘊，說明色蘊的各種差別相，又分二十九科；第一科有色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：於諸蘊中，何義、幾蘊是有色？答：即以此性還說此性，色自性義是有色義。一蘊是有色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理名有色？有幾蘊是有色？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：以色法本身的特性來說明有色的道理，色本身的自性是有色義。五蘊中的色蘊一蘊是屬於有色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、有見</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科有見，說明有見的定義及五蘊中屬於有見法的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有見？答：眼所行義。一蘊一分是有見。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理名有見？有幾蘊是有見？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼所活動的境界；眼根所取，眼識所緣的境界，就是有見。五蘊中色蘊這一蘊，其中的一部分如色聲香味觸屬於眼識所緣取的色，就是有見色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、有對2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科有對，說明有對的定義及五蘊中屬於有對法的種類，分二科；第一科問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有對？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，哪些道理說名有對？有幾蘊是有對？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、釋義2　巳一、標二種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科釋義，解釋有對的意思，又分二科；第一科標二種，標出二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4489"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：展轉相觸據處所義及麤大義，是有對義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：二法之間彼此可以展轉互相地接觸，佔有空間，以及麤大的色法，是有對義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著比較困難的地方解釋一下，解釋麤的定義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">麤大義者，當知遠離三種微細。此三微細，如前應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　麤大義，應當知道遠離三種微細性就是麤大義。這三種微細性，如前文所說應知。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 損減微細性，分析麤色至極微位就是損減微細性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 種類微細性，是指風等色及中有色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 心自在轉微細性，是指色界、無色二界由定自在所生的色法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離這三種微細性，就是麤大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一蘊一分是有對。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有對是指色蘊這一蘊中，有一部分的色法是有對；這一部分是色蘊中的十色處屬於有對。有對義不會超過三種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、 相觸對：能夠觸對的色法，簡別不是中有色及定自在所生色，因這二種色法不會互相觸對；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、 極麤顯：很麤顯的色法，簡別不是風等色及色界由業所生報色，因為這二類色法都非常微細；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、 據處所：有體積占據空間，是眼識所取的色境。諸色皆是有對。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》此三微細如前應知者：前說：微細性略有三種。一、損減微細性，二、種類微細性，三、心自在轉微細性。如彼別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/54.htm#44088:42242">陵本五十四卷十一頁4327</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　卷54，1781頁說微細性要略而言有三種：損減微細性就是指極微；種類微細性就是指風及中有；心自在轉微細性是指色界色或者是無色界的定自在所生色，這些色法都很微細。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、有漏2　卯一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科有漏，說明有漏的定義及五蘊中屬於有漏法的種類，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有漏？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名有漏？有幾蘊是有漏？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、答2　辰一、略標簡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，要略的標示簡別出來，分二科；第一科略標簡，要略標示簡別有漏法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：麤重所隨，非彼對治，煩惱所生義。一切一分是有漏。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：麤重是煩惱品的種子，若是若異熟品所攝，及餘無記品所攝，唯名麤重不名隨眠；若信等善法品所攝種子，不名麤重，也不名隨眠。五蘊常為煩惱種子所隨逐，煩惱種子在沒有被對治以前，都有可能生起煩惱的現行。在五蘊中除少部分是無漏的，以及少部分的情形通於有漏無漏外，幾乎都是屬於有漏。一切五蘊中有煩惱種子隨逐，由煩惱所生的五蘊都是有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《大乘阿毘達磨雜集論》卷3〈1 三法品〉說：「五取蘊十五界十處全及三界二處少分是有漏。謂除最後三界二處少分聖道眷屬及諸無為，非有漏故。為捨執著漏合我故。觀察有漏。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4490"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》麤重所隨等者：謂於識蘊，煩惱種子未害未斷，是名麤重所隨。於彼煩惱非能對治，從彼一切煩惱而生，是名非彼對治煩惱所生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在阿賴耶識中的煩惱種子，沒有被禪定損伏，也沒有被無漏的聖道所斷除，名麤重所隨。由於有煩惱種子，修聖道沒有堪能性，剛強難調，好像人的身體很笨重，也是麤重。煩惱種子沒有被對治過，由煩惱所產生的五蘊，屬於有漏法，是名非彼對治煩惱所生。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、廣餘義4　巳一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣餘義，再詳細解釋有漏的其他定義，分四科；第一科標，標出有漏義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有有漏義，謂若是處煩惱能生四種過失，是有漏義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於有漏又有其他的解釋，當內心有煩惱，有貪瞋癡時，會有四種過失，這個時候就是有漏，將功德漏掉了。關於這一段文可以配合本論卷65所說由五相故，建立有漏諸法差別，加以思惟。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五相是：由事故、隨眠故、相應故、所緣故、生起故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由事故，是指有漏法事，包括清淨內色，及彼相依（根所依處）不相依外色（外色聲等），若諸染汙心心所，若善、無記心心所等。這有漏法事，由隨其所應，由餘隨眠、相應、所緣、生起四相說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、隨眠相，若於清淨諸色，及於如前所說一切心心所中，煩惱種子未害未斷，說名隨眠，亦名麤重。若彼乃至未無餘斷，當知一切由隨眠故，說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、相應相，若諸染汙心心所，由相應故，說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、所緣相，若諸有事，若現量所行，若有漏所生增上所起，如是一切漏所緣故，名為有漏。此中現在，名為有事；過去、未來，名非有事。若依清淨色識所行，名現量所行；若餘所行，當知名非現量所行。若內諸處增上生起一切外處，名有漏所生增上所起。唯彼所緣當知有漏。所以者何？若緣去來起諸煩惱，過去、未來非有事故，不由所緣說名有漏。若現在事非現量所行，如清淨色，及一切染汙、善、無記心心所，彼亦非煩惱所緣故，說名有漏。但由自分別所起相，起諸煩惱，非彼諸法為此分明所行境故。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、生起相，又分二種</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、約諸法辨，諸隨眠未永斷故，順煩惱境現在前故，於彼現起不如理作意故。由此因緣，諸所有法正生、已生、或復當生，如是一切，由生起故，說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2.、約欲界繫辨，又從一切不善煩惱諸異熟果（欲界諸異熟果），及異熟果增上所引外事生起，如是一切，亦生起故，說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、約色無色繫辨，又由無記色無色繫一切煩惱，於彼續生；彼所續生，亦生起故，說名有漏。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是名為由五相故，建立有漏諸法差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為四種過失？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是四種過失？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出四種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、不寂靜過失，二、內外變異過失，三、發起惡行過失，四、攝受因過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、不寂靜過失：煩惱的相貌就是不寂靜，心裡有煩惱時，會感覺很煩躁或是鬱悶，行住坐臥都不安。本論〈有尋有伺等三地〉卷8，221頁說：「若法生時其相自然不寂靜起，由彼起故，不寂靜行相續而轉，是名略說煩惱自性。」《瑜伽師地論略纂》卷3說：「身心相續，不寂靜轉，是煩惱相」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、內外變異過失：有煩惱以後，內根與外塵都會產生變化，心裡又隨逐著內根與外塵生起更多煩惱，產生過失。《大明三藏法數》卷13說：諸眾生由內心亂想，外境遷流，心境相應，更互變異，所謂心隨境起，境逐心生，煩惱纏綿，不能解脫，是為內外變異過失。　</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、發起惡行過失：煩惱生時就容易發起惡行，造作種種惡業。《大明三藏法數》卷13說：諸眾生由煩惱妄惑，造諸殺盜婬妄種種惡業，輪轉生死，無有出期，是為發起惡行過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、攝受因過失：有了煩惱就會引生下一個果報體，這個果報體又會與煩惱相應，因此不要輕易起煩惱，一起煩惱，就熏入阿賴耶識中，下一生遇緣就要受果報。《大明三藏法數》卷13說：「謂諸眾生由造種種惡業之因，攝取未來苦果展轉輪迴，不能解脫，是為攝受因過失。」煩惱是無量無邊的，要斷煩惱極不容易，一天二十四小時，心念那麼多，心能覺察得到的只是少分，很多都漏掉了。古代大德教我們，想一想每天從早到晚，幾個念頭是好的？幾個念頭是在色聲香味觸上轉？自己檢查一下，就知道自己會在哪一界受生了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋煩惱所產生的四種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知初過失，纏現行所作；第二過失，諸煩惱事隨逐煩惱所作；第三過失，煩惱因緣所作；第四過失，引發後有所作。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知第一個不寂靜的過失，由於煩惱現行所造作成的，煩惱起時像一條繩子牢牢綁住我們。第二內外變異過失，諸煩惱事是指煩惱所依的根身，所緣的器世間，隨順煩惱而有種種的變異。第三發起惡行過失，這是由於煩惱的因緣所引起的造作。第四攝受因過失，由煩惱引發後有，得到下一生果報體，煩惱是得到來生果報體的生因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》諸煩惱事隨逐煩惱所作者：謂有取蘊內外諸事，是名諸煩惱事。彼為煩惱之所隨逐，由是因緣，能生內外變異過失，是名隨逐煩惱所作。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由煩惱的取著而招感的五蘊內根、外塵，就是諸煩惱事。這些五蘊內根、外塵的煩惱事又被煩惱所隨逐，由這些因緣，內根、外塵會有種種變化的過失，稱為隨逐煩惱所作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、有為</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科有為，說明有為的定義及五蘊中屬於有為法的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4491"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有為？答：從因已生及應生義。一切是有為。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名有為？有幾蘊是有為的？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由過去業因已經生出現行的五蘊，及應該生出來的五蘊法，這一切都是有為法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、有諍</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科有諍，有漏的異名是有諍，說明有諍的定義及五蘊中屬於有諍的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有諍？答：多隨瞋恚自在轉義。一切一分是有諍。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名有諍？有幾蘊是有諍？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：有煩惱就有諍，身語意多分隨瞋恚轉時名有諍，五蘊中一分多隨瞋恚自在轉者，稱為有諍。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、有愛味</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科有愛味，說明有愛味的定義及五蘊中屬於有愛味的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是有愛味？答：多隨愛見自在轉義。一切一分是有愛味。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名有愛味？有幾蘊是有愛味？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：當五蘊多分隨愛見煩惱而轉時，愛著自身世間，愛味執著自己的思想。一切五蘊中一分多隨愛見自在轉就稱為有愛味。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除了阿羅漢或八地以上的菩薩或佛，已完全斷了煩惱的聖人以外，都是有愛味，所以說除了無漏的聖人外，一切五蘊中是有愛味，稱為一切一分是有愛味。可以檢查一下自己的五蘊，是有諍？有愛味？還是無漏的？有愛味其實是通於三界，欲界的人對於欲有愛味；色界的人對於色界定有愛味；無色界的人對於無色界定有愛味，三界眾生都是有愛味。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、依耽嗜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科依耽嗜，說明依耽嗜的定義及五蘊中屬於依耽嗜的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是依耽嗜？答：多隨欲貪自在轉義。一切一分是依耽嗜。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名依耽嗜？有幾蘊是依耽嗜？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：多分隨順欲貪，生起欲貪時，一切五蘊中多隨欲貪自在轉這一分，就稱為依耽嗜。欲貪通常是指對欲界色聲香味觸男女的染污心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅九、世間</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科世間，說明世間的定義及五蘊中屬於世間的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是世間？答：戲論依義。一切一分是世間。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名世間？有幾蘊是世間？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：生起世間戲論的所依根及所緣境名世間。一切一分是世間，這是指有漏五蘊，依止五蘊產生種種戲論分別，這都是屬於世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷65說：由五相故建立世間諸法差別。包括：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、一切清淨色及清淨所取色世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、一切染污心心所世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、一切無記心心所世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、一切善心心所若當斷若已斷世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、一切世間三摩地所行無見無對色世間。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又說依五種世間，即彼世間名墮諸法，謂有情世間、器世間、欲世間、色世間、無色世間，當知是名五種世間。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十、墮界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科墮界，說明墮界的定義及五蘊中屬於墮界的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是墮界？答：三界所攝世間義。一切一分是墮界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名墮界？有幾蘊是墮界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：欲界、色界、無色界所攝的有情世間、器世間及五蘊世間名墮界。一切五蘊中的一分，如果和三界的戲論相應的話，都是屬於墮界。心如果沒有在佛法上，失去正念正知時，通常多分生起欲界的戲論。若修定時，也可能是色界定、或者無色界定，這時都是屬於墮界所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷65，2103頁說到墮界作意所緣諸法：「欲界繫善染污無記作意，緣一切三界諸法；色界繫善作意，亦緣一切三界諸法；無色界中若定若生，外道異生無色界繫善作意，唯緣自地一切法，非下地。若毘鉢舍那行菩薩未得自在，及有廣慧聲聞乘等，若諸有學若阿羅漢，彼無色界繫善作意，亦緣下地一切法；若諸菩薩已得自在，決定不於無色界生，由觀於彼不能現起利眾生事因此成熟廣大佛法，及能成熟利益有情行故，當知是名墮界作意所緣諸法。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十一、過去</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十一科過去，說明過去的定義及五蘊中屬於過去的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4492"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="67605:44120"></a><a name="67500:44120"></a>問：何義、幾蘊是過去？答：已受用因果義。一切是過去。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名過去？有幾蘊是過去？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：已經得到受用的因及果，即諸法自相已生已滅名為過去。一切五蘊當中，若已經得到受用的因及果名為過去，此處是約現在五蘊假立三世差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十二、未來</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十二科未來，說明未來的定義及五蘊中屬於未來的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是未來？答：未受用因果義。一切是未來。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名未來？有幾蘊是未來？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：還沒有受用因的果法，就是未來。一切是未來，約現在五蘊含攝未來因法，名一切五蘊是未來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十三、現在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十三科現在，說明現在的定義及五蘊中屬於現在的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是現在？答：已受用因義及未受用果義。一切是現在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名現在？有幾蘊是現在？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：若諸法已經受用到因了，現在的五蘊是過去業因所招感的，現前的造作立即熏成種子，但新熏的種子還沒有得到未來的果，這一切是現在的五蘊。當下的五蘊，也有過去、也有現在、也有未來。所以說一剎那就是永劫，有這樣的意趣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處為什麼這樣安立？因為過去與未來無體，唯現在法有。於不存在的法，還討論它作什麼？這就是告訴我們，在現在的五蘊裡面，可以看到過去的因果，果報體是過去因的呈現；現行五蘊就屬於現在，現在的五蘊又熏下未來的因。一剎那中具足過去、現在、未來，故此處說五蘊同時是過去、也是現在、也是未來。為什麼要觀察五蘊的過去、現在、未來？因為我們一直在執著有一個我在流轉，現在告訴我們，過去的不是我，現在也不是我，未來也不是我，都不是我，只是因緣和合暫時的幻現而已，本論一直提醒我們「無我」的道理。這些分別在表面上看起來很瑣碎，但每一個分別都是要我們契入五蘊是無我的真實義，因為五蘊有各種不同的型態出現，我也是以不同的相貌呈現，論主從不同的相貌來分析五蘊，告訴我們，那個相貌不是我。這樣說起來，本論整部幾乎是一部大的無我觀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無著菩薩也說，為什麼要造這部論，還要分別那麼多？因為這是一切種智的因，如果要成佛，很多事情都要知道，必須法門無量誓願學，知道這麼多，才能契入一切種智。這些都是毗鉢舍那，由觀能幫助止，如果要修止，也是相應的，為什麼？因為已經對於所緣境生起決擇慧，心止於此，不再被動搖，相續成片就是止了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　藕益大師《成唯識論觀心法要》卷3說：因果等言，皆（依增益相似而）假施設。觀現在法有引後用，假立當果，對說現因；觀現在法有酬前相，假立曾因，對說現果。假，謂於現在識上。似彼當果曾因之相而現，如是因果總不離現前一剎那法，理趣顯然，遠離斷常二邊，契會中道，諸有智者，應順修學。祇是現前一剎那法，望前即名為果，望後即名為因。約現在果，談過去因，則塵點劫前，猶若今日，乃于現識變似過去因相，而非實緣過去事也，以過去已滅，無可緣故；約現在因，記未來果，則無量劫後，猶如指掌，乃於現識變似未來果相，而非實緣未來事也，以未來未生，無可緣故。所以說；十世古今，始終不離於當念。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十四、內</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十四科內，說明內的定義及五蘊中屬於內的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是內？答：六處并屬彼義。一蘊一分、四蘊全是內。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名內？有幾蘊是屬於內？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：六處以及屬於六處相應之法名內。內就是指根身，還有加上受想行識四蘊。色蘊中的五色根之扶根塵及內身這一部分，加上受想行識四蘊的全部名內。色蘊中屬於外的色聲香味觸，就不屬於內了；行者應當觀察內身不是我，內受想行識不是我。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》六處并屬彼義等者：眼等六處，及彼所屬諸所有法，內事攝故，建立名內。色蘊一分，受、想、行、識四蘊全，是內法類。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六處，及六處所屬諸所有法，都屬於內事所攝，建立名內。色蘊的五根這一部分，加上受想行識四蘊全部，都是屬於內法類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十五、外</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十五科外，說明外的定義及五蘊中屬於外的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是外？答：內相違義。一蘊一分是外。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有哪些道理說名外？有幾蘊是屬於外？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：和內法相違的就稱為外。一蘊一分是外，色蘊中不屬於有情的五塵，色聲香味觸，就是屬於外了。行者應觀外身非身，非我，是名外身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十六、麤</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十六科麤，說明麤的定義及五蘊中屬於麤的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4493"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="11360:44133"></a>問：何義、幾蘊是麤？答：不光潔積聚相增長義。一切一分是麤。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有哪些道理說名麤？有幾蘊是屬於麤？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：麤是指蘊不光潔，是由積聚而有的有對色，相增長是包括色、無色蘊的相狀增長名麤；五蘊中有一部分如果屬於這種特性稱為麤。《瑜伽論記》說：三惡趣的五蘊就是屬於麤義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》不光潔積聚相增長義者：欲界繫色，不光潔攝。諸有對色，積聚所攝。色無色蘊長養等流，相增長攝。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　繫屬於欲界的色法，是不光潔的，是麤色；諸多有質礙的色法，屬於積聚的色法，也可以稱為麤；色無色蘊有飲食、睡眠、梵行等長養等流時，如色相康強，心力增長時，屬於相增長所攝，也可以稱為麤。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十七、細</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十七科細，說明細的定義及五蘊中屬於細的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是細？答：麤相違義。一切一分是細。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有哪些道理說名細？有幾蘊是屬於細？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：與麤義相違的，就是細，換句話說，不是麤的就是細的。五蘊中有一部分是屬於細。《瑜伽論記》說：欲界人天的五蘊，如果和三惡趣比起來，三惡道的五蘊是麤，欲界人天的五蘊是細。若欲界與色界、無色界比起來，欲界的五蘊是麤，色界無色界的五蘊是細。麤細是觀待而有，並非有真實的麤細。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十八、劣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十八科劣，說明劣的定義及五蘊中屬於劣的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是劣？答：無常、苦、不淨、染汙義。一切一分是劣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名劣？有幾蘊是屬於劣的？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：若是屬於無常、苦、不淨而且是染污的五蘊就屬於劣。除了無漏的五蘊這一分之外，所有有漏的五蘊都是屬於劣的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十九、妙</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十九科妙，說明妙的定義及五蘊中屬於妙的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是妙？答：劣相違義。一切一分是妙。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名妙？有幾蘊是屬於妙？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：與劣相違的屬性，不是無常、不是苦、不染污的都是妙。一切五蘊有一部分是妙。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《雜集論》說，無漏的五蘊就是屬於妙。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二十、遠</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十科遠，說明遠的定義及五蘊中屬於遠的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是遠？答：處所、去來、時、方隔越義。一切一分是遠。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名遠？有幾蘊是屬於遠？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：處所之間的距離很遠，或者去來的時間上很遠，這類時間、空間上有所阻隔有障礙時稱為遠。過去、未來的五蘊這一部分可以說都是屬於遠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》處所去來時方隔越義者：遠有二義，一者、處遠，二者、時遠。謂若諸處方所隔越，是名處遠，當知此唯依色蘊有。又若去來時分隔越，是名時遠，當知此通色無色蘊。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠有二個意思，第一、處所遠，第二、時間遠。若是處所隔得很遠的地方，稱為處遠，應當了知這是依色蘊而安立。若過去未來在時間上相隔得很遠，稱作時遠，應當了知這是通於色無色蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4494"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二十一、近</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十一科近，說明近的定義及五蘊中屬於近的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是近？答：遠相違義。一切一分是近。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名近？有幾蘊是屬於近？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：與遠相違，時空上沒有阻隔障礙就是近。現在的五蘊這一部分是近，過去生、或未來生的五蘊名遠。行者應當觀察不論是過去、未來、現在，若遠若近的五蘊，都是無我的，也不是我所有的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二十二、三界繫2　卯一、第一義3　辰一、欲界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十二科三界繫，說明三界繫的定義及五蘊中屬於三界繫的種類，分二科；第一科第一義，由第一個道理觀察三界，又分三科；第一科欲界繫，說明欲界繫的定義及五蘊中屬於欲界繫的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是欲界繫？答：於此間生，未得對治；或得已出，三時現行義。一切一分是欲界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名欲界繫？有幾蘊是屬於欲界繫？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：此間是指欲界，在欲界受生的五蘊，而且沒有被禪定或聖道對治過；或者得到禪定或聖道，成就色界心或無漏法，又從禪定或聖道出來，過去、現在、未來三時現行的欲界五蘊及所依器世間，稱為欲界繫。一切五蘊中屬於上述情形中的一分是欲界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66說：「云何欲界繫法？謂於欲界若生、若長未離欲界欲，心不在定，於此位中所有諸法，或生得故或作意故，已行正行當行，是名欲界繫法。」</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於此間生等者：謂若身生欲界，未得色界定地對治；或復得已，從彼定出。於爾所時，彼所有蘊，去來今位剎那流轉，當知彼蘊是欲界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　屬於欲界繫是什麼情況？如果一個人生在欲界，沒有得到色界定；或者是得到定，從色界定出來，在那個時間內，所有的五蘊及器世間，於過去、未來、現在剎那剎那相續流轉，這樣的五蘊是屬於欲界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、色界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色界繫，說明色界繫的定義及五蘊中屬於色界繫的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是色界繫？答：已得色界繫對治，若入彼定；或復生彼，未得上對治；或得已出，三時現行義。一切一分是色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名色界繫？有幾蘊是屬於色界繫？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：以欲界身得到色界定及入色界定時，成就色界繫有漏種子；或者是受生於色界，還沒有得無色界定，在那個時間內，所有的五蘊及器世間，於過去、未來、現在剎那剎那相續現行，這樣的五蘊是屬於色界繫。一切五蘊中屬於上述情形中的一分是色界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈決擇‧思所成慧地〉卷66說：「復次云何色界繫法？謂生欲界能現證入隨一靜慮，已離欲界欲，未離色界欲，未發上加行（即無色界定），或從彼定（無色界定）起（回到色界定），所有世間意地諸法，依意識入色界世間靜慮，由定地作意，包括已經入定、正在入定、將要入定的意識活動，名為色界繫法；或生色界（天）未離彼欲，未發上加行，或生得故或作意故，諸世間法已行正行當行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》未得上對治者：此說無色界繫定地對治，名上對治應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，還沒有得到無色界定，還沒有對治色界欲，稱為上對治。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、無色界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無色界繫，說明無色界繫的定義及五蘊中屬於無色界繫的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是無色界繫？答：已得無色界繫對治，若入彼定；或復生彼，未得上對治；或得已出，三時現行義。一切一分是無色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名無色界繫？有幾蘊是屬於無色界繫？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：欲界或色界有情，已經得到無色界定，入無色界定，成就無色界繫有漏種子；或者生在無色界天，可是還沒有得到出世間離欲的上對治道，還沒有成就聖道，具有無色四蘊；或者是已經得到上對治道的無漏定，又從無漏定裡面出來，在那個時間內，諸蘊於過去、未來、現在剎那剎那相續現行，這種蘊屬於無色界繫。一切五蘊中屬於上述情形中的一分是無色界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4495"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》未得上對治者：此說出世離欲，名上對治應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知，此處是說出世離欲，名為上對治。五蘊隨時有可能屬於欲界、可能色界、可能無色界，而三界都是內心的虛妄分別，觀破三界心的因緣性、無常性、苦性、無我性、欺誑性，無所得、無所有才能離三界欲，得上對治。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、第二義3　辰一、欲界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，依第二個解釋來簡別三界，分三科；第一科欲界繫，從第二個道理說明欲界繫法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。謂輕安俱三摩地及彼眷屬并彼果法所不攝義，是欲界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有另一種道理說名欲界繫，就是除了輕安俱的三摩地及彼眷屬的心心所法，以及定境果色之外，其餘的都是欲界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《瑜伽論記》卷15說：此處說輕安俱三摩地，是簡別不是散心三摩地。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眷屬並果，景法師說：這是指與輕安俱三摩地同時之善五蘊名眷屬；若定及眷屬所生異熟名彼果法。窺基大師說：眷屬是指與定同時心心所法；彼果法，是指定共戒、或道共戒及定境果色，於此安立色界等繫，其餘屬欲界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》輕安俱三摩地等者：輕安一法唯定地有，故三摩地名輕安俱。諸靜慮支為依緣等，名彼眷屬。從定所生諸功德法，名彼果法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　只有定地才有輕安。從未到地定到初禪、二禪、三禪、四禪，都可以稱為輕安俱三摩地。靜慮的支分，如初禪尋、伺、喜、樂、心一境性，尋、伺為入定所依，心一境性為入定所緣，喜、樂為得定功德，這些都稱為禪定眷屬。從定裡面產生種種的功德，如定共戒及伏除欲恚害等，就是定的果法。如初禪如是二、三、四禪也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、色界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科色界繫，以第二個道理說明色界繫法。根據心所法來定位。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">屬色煩惱、與彼相違所攝義，是色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　屬於色界的煩惱，色界有漏諸法從色界的煩惱而生。色界還有愛、見、慢、疑的煩惱，這些與色界相應的煩惱，與欲界相違反，名為色界繫。第二個義就是根據心所法來定位欲界、色界、無色界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》與彼相違所攝義者：謂與前說欲界繫法相違，屬色煩惱之所攝故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　與彼相違所攝是指與前說欲界繫法不同，屬於色界煩惱之所攝。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、無色界繫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無色界繫，以第二個道理說明無色界繫法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">離色煩惱、彼所攝義，當知是無色界繫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　遠離色界的煩惱，還有無色界的煩惱，從無色界的煩惱所生諸有漏法，是無色界繫。與無色界繫煩惱相應的四蘊，也是無色界繫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二十三、三性2　卯一、第一義3　辰一、善</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二十三科三性，說明三性的定義及五蘊中屬於三性的種類，三性是善性、惡性、無記性，由二道理說明，分二科；第一科第一義，先用第一道理說明三性法，又分三科；第一科善，說明善性的定義及五蘊中屬於善性的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是善？答：能感當來樂果報義，及煩惱苦永斷對治義。一切一分是善。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有哪些道理說名善？有幾蘊是屬於善法？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：善的定義很多，能夠感得將來可愛果報的有漏善，以及無漏善能夠對治及永遠斷除煩惱及苦，說名為善。五蘊中的一部分相應於有漏善或無漏善的這一分，名善五蘊。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4496"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、不善</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不善，說明不善性的定義及五蘊中屬於不善性的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是不善？答：能感當來苦果報義，及能發起諸惡行義。一切一分是不善。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有哪些道理說名不善？有幾蘊是屬於不善法？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：能夠感得將來三惡道的苦惱果報，而且能夠產生種種邪惡的行為，稱為惡。五蘊的一部分如果與根本煩惱、隨煩惱相應時，名不善。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、無記</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無記，說明無記性的定義及五蘊中屬於無記性的種類。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何義、幾蘊是無記？答：彼俱相違義。一切一分是無記。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：在五蘊當中，有什麼道理說名無記？有幾蘊是屬於無記法？</span></span></span></div>
