<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前蘊善巧中，已廣分別有色、無色，乃至無斷等義。此十八界隨順蘊善巧的廣分別義，應更建立十八界的諸門分別，比照蘊善巧的諸義，應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、依勝義世俗辨2　寅一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依勝義世俗辨，分別十八界的四種義，其中第一科，依勝義道理或世俗道理，說明十八界的情況，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：如說眼見諸色乃至意了諸法，此為眼等是見者乃至是了者耶？為彼識耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如說眼看到色塵，乃至意了別諸法，那麼眼等是見者乃至意等是了別者嗎？還是眼識在見乃至意識在了別？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答2　卯一、明勝義2　辰一、標非</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科明勝義，約勝義道理來說，標出不是眼等，又分二科；第一科標非，標出也不是彼識是見者等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：約勝義道理，非是眼等，亦非彼識。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：如果以勝義諦的道理來說，既不是眼見色，也不是眼識見色。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4523"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋由</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋由，解釋理由。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？諸法自性眾緣生故，剎那滅故，無作用故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？因為這一切法現前，如眼見色等事，要由眾緣所生，就像前面說的，眼識的生起，必須還要有所依根，所緣境、助伴心所、作業等五法和合運轉，眼見色這件事才會產生，因緣具足諸法才能現行。諸法現行之後剎那就滅，沒有真實的作用，無有一法真實存在過，故不能說是眼見色，還是眼識見色。這是由勝義諦道理來看的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、顯世俗3　辰一、標最勝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯世俗，約世俗諦的道理來說，分三科；第一科標最勝，標出最殊勝的那一點來說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">約世俗道理，眼等最勝，故可於彼立見者等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約世間的道理來說，以世間人共同的認知而言，眼等根識與見色等有最勝的功能，那麼就假安立為眼見色、耳聞聲、鼻嗅香、舌嚐味、身覺觸、意知法等，說眼等是見者乃至是意是了者，或識是見者乃至了者等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋所以</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋為什麼這樣說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？若有眼等諸根，識決定生。無所闕減，或有識流；非眼等根若闕不闕，俱可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？因為若有眼等諸根，依根緣境眼等諸識決定能生，若無諸根不能發識，事實上真的能了別色塵的，還是心識而不是根，但是因為有眼根才可能有眼識，所以我們就說眼見色，乃至耳聞聲等。這是依於最勝所依的道理。或有一種情形，無論眼等根闕或不闕，識流的相續都一直存在，識種子的相續不會因為根壞掉，就沒有了。有些人的眼根壞掉，換了眼角膜，還可以再看，因為識種子沒有壞掉，不因為根不在，而識種子就不在。由此可知若有眼等根就能生眼等識，若根缺不現行，識種並未斷滅，遇緣仍可現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、明安立</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明安立，說明見者的安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此中實義，唯於見等說見者等。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這裡真實的道理，是要我們這樣觀想，唯於見色等說見者等，離見等之外，沒有其他的見者存在。見色聞聲不是我在那裡見色聞聲，而是眼等根識在那裡活動。由勝義道理，見色即非見色是名見色，見色等也無真實作用，諸法唯是內心的虛妄分別，行者若能常作如是觀察，就能契入無我的真實義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》無所闕減或有識流等者：眼等諸根不滅壞故，是名無闕；不羸劣故，是名無減。由此無所闕減，定相續故，能為眼等諸識最勝所依。是故或時有識流轉，名有識流。非眼等根若闕不闕，彼有識流，俱可得故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果眼等六根沒有壞滅時，說名無闕。諸根沒有羸弱衰減，說名無減。由眼等六根沒有闕減，決定相續，能為眼等諸識最勝所依，能生六識。有時候因緣具足根境和合，就有識依根現前活動，名為有識流。並不是眼等根若闕或不闕，識流都是可得的；根壞時，識即不能現行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、次第分別2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科次第分別，廣分別十八界的最後一科次第分別，以次第分別十八界，分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4524"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：此十八界，幾種次第宣說因緣？此復何等？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：十八界有幾種次第宣說的因緣？內容又是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標列，標示列舉出有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：略有二種。一、三種次第宣說因緣，二、六種次第宣說因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：十八界為什麼要這樣安立，要略而言有二種道理。一種是三種的次第宣說因緣，另一種是六種的次第宣說因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、隨釋2　卯一、三種因緣2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著解釋，分二科；第一科三種因緣，先說三種因緣，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何三種次第宣說因緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為三種次第宣說因緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、標差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標差別，標示約所依、境界、俱依差別而安立十八界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂所依、境界、俱依差別故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以三種次第宣說十八界因緣，是以諸識所依的六根界，所緣的六塵境界，及俱依的六識差別，而安立六根界、六塵界、六識界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著比較難懂的地方解釋一下。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？由識與根同一處義，故說名依；境界是所緣義，故亦名依。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？由於識與根同在一個處所，而說名依；境界是識的所緣，所以也是依。依根緣境才能發識，因此識就是俱依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》所依境界俱依差別者：眼等六根是名所依，色等六境是名境界，眼等六識是名俱依。識望依、緣，俱名依故，如下自釋。然此名依，是能依義，識依根、境而得轉故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼耳鼻舌身意六根，名為所依。色聲香味觸法是六種境界，眼等六識的生起需要依止所依根與境界，因此識名為俱依；識對望於所依根，以及所緣境，都稱為依止，如下文解釋。然而俱依這個依是指能依，因為六識能依六根、六境，而得生起現行作用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4525"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、六種因緣2　辰一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科六種因緣，說明由六種因緣安立十八界的次第，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何六種次第宣說因緣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是由六種次第宣說十八界的因緣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋2　巳一、長行2　午一、別說眼等6　未一、依所行差別辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科長行，以長行敘述，又分二科；第一科別說眼等，各別的說眼耳鼻舌身意等，又分六科；第一科依所行差別辨，依五根活動的所緣境有多少，來安立十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂彼所行眾多差別數數行故，先說眼等。是初因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以第一個因緣，說明為什麼先安立眼界、耳界、鼻界、舌界、身界的次第。這是以諸根活動的所緣境多少有差別而安立的。五根中眼所見色最多，耳於所聞聲較少，所以先說眼，次說耳，如是乃至身等，這是第一個以所緣多少安立十八界次第的因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂彼所行眾多差別等者：當知此約眼等五根為論，說彼次第。意地中說：屢觀眾色，觀而復捨，故名為眼。數數於此聲至能聞，故名為耳。數由此故能齅諸香，故名為鼻。能除饑羸、數發言論、表彰呼召，故名為舌。諸根所隨，周遍積聚，故名為身。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/03.htm#44495:2441">陵本三卷十五頁254</a>）其義應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知這是以五根來說安立十八界的次第。〈本地分‧意地〉卷1，105頁中說：眼的定義是一次又一次的觀察色法，觀了以後就不再看了，五根中眼睛所見色最多，所以先說眼。一次又一次聲音到了能夠聽到，這是耳；每一次出現香的因緣時，能夠嗅到，這種功能稱作鼻；能除去身體的飢餓羸劣，表達彰顯內心的思想，用種種名字來召呼各種事物，這種功能稱作舌；眼耳鼻舌四根隨逐依附於此，遍滿全身，整個這一大塊都都是身根。這是卷3所說應當了知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未二、依世間俗事辨3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依世間俗事辨，第二個因緣，依止世間俗事安立十八界次第，分三科；第一科標，標示出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又隨世間俗事轉故，說彼次第。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又隨順世間的俗事，世間人作事時是怎麼樣活動，是依活動的過程來安立十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由諸世間先互相見，次相慰問，次設飲食，次過晝分夜分現前，敷設種種軟妙臥具氈蓐被枕，觸習侍女。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於世間人互相見面時，先用眼睛看到對方，因此先說眼界；再出聲互相招呼慰問，故次說耳界；接著施設飲食招待吃飯，此時鼻子嗅到香噴噴的飯菜，舉箸用餐以舌品嚐佳餚，接著安立鼻界、舌界；吃完飯，太陽下山白天已過，夜幕低垂，沐浴淨身之後，舖設種種柔軟舒適的微妙臥具和氈蓐棉被、枕頭及侍女伺候，還要身觸這些事情，最後安立身界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4526"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是第二因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是第二因緣，隨順世間俗事的過程，安立十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又隨世間俗事轉故等者：當知此約色等五境為論，說彼次第，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以世間俗事的色聲香味觸等五境而論，說明色聲香味觸的次第，如文中所說可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未三、依喜樂差別辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依喜樂差別辨，說明第三種因緣，依喜樂差別安立十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又喜樂差別為依止故，次第宣說。是第三因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這一段文引《瑜伽論記》景法師說：隨諸佛菩薩喜樂故，而安立十八界次第。窺基大師說：這是以有情內心對境的歡喜好樂而安立，一般有情都歡喜眼見諸色等，依此安立十八界次第。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛說法有三種方式，一隨自意語，根據佛的智慧而說，如為欲界眾生說，父母即是身因，或一切眾生悉有佛性，或一切眾生不斷不滅乃至得阿耨多羅三藐三菩提，或自所證一實相等，都名隨自意說，若佛隨自意而說時，除佛無人能夠測知。二隨他意語，稱合眾生根機，一向方便引導眾生而說，非究竟之說，若佛隨他意而說，乃至昆蟲也能了知。三隨自他意語，一半宣說自證，一半隨眾生根機而說。如一切世間智者說有，佛也說有；智人說無，佛也說無，世間智人說五欲樂有無常苦無我可斷，佛也說有；世間智人說五欲樂有常我淨無有是處，佛也如是說無是處，這是佛隨三世智人所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》喜樂差別為依止故者：此亦約彼色等五境為論。依彼色等喜樂生故，勝劣有別，故次第說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這也是以色聲香味觸五境而言，依止色等所生內心的喜樂有殊勝、下劣的差別，就這樣次第安立。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未四、依嚴飾差別辨3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依嚴飾差別辨，說明第四個因緣依莊嚴修飾身相差別安立十八界次第，分三科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又嚴飾差別所攝受故，次第宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依有情莊嚴修飾身相差別，而安立眼等十八界次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">諸受欲者，必以安繕那等先莊眉眼，次以耳璫、耳輪等莊嚴其耳，非於餘根。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　安繕那，是一種印度的藥石，顏色是青黑色粉墨，可以用來畫眼影。世間受欲的人，化妝時喜歡在眼睛上面畫藍色、或黑色眼影；眼睛畫好了，要掛耳環、耳璫（穿耳施珠曰璫，即掛在耳朵上的寶珠）等莊嚴她的耳朵，不是在鼻子、舌頭或身上掛。因為這個次第，先來化妝眼睛，然後再掛耳環，就用眼耳鼻舌身來說十八界的次第。可見佛陀不但善知法相、善說法，世間事也是很通達。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4527"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是嚴飾，是第四因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如此依莊嚴修飾身相差別，是安立十八界次第的第四個因緣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》嚴飾差別所攝受故等者：此約眼、耳次第為論，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是依於女人化妝先眼、次耳的次第來說的，如文所說可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未五、依作業等事辨3　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科依作業等事辨，說明第五個因緣依世間人的作業次第，而宣說十八界的次第，分三科；第一科標，標示出。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依作業、飲食、習欲等事，次第宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依世間人所做的事，吃飯，還有習欲，有欲就是要有觸，這些事情的次第來宣說十八界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由諸眾生皆先依止身語二業若淨不淨方便勤求，次食段食；既飽醉已，習近諸欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由世間人都先依止身語二種業，動身發語勤造作淨不淨業追求生活所需，其次一日三餐維持生命，飽暖思淫欲，所以習近諸欲。依世間人做事、吃飯、習欲之日常生活而安立十八界次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是第五因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是第五個因緣，依世間人作業、飲食、習欲等事的次第來安立十八界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又依作業飲食等者：此中約彼色等五境為論，說彼次第，如文可知。為作業等之所依止，名依作業、飲食、習欲等事。言身語二業若淨不淨者，義顯色、聲通善不善。由軟中上品三種思差別故，能起若善不善身語表業，義如前說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/54.htm#44522:42680">陵本五十四卷十九頁4366</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是以色聲香味觸五境來說次第，如文可知。身就是色，語就是聲，段食就是香、味，習欲是觸。世間人造業時，要依止身、語業，然後又有飲食、習欲等事。身語二業若淨不淨，是指身所依色，語所依聲通善不善，由思心所造作時有軟中上品三種差別，能發起善或不善的身語表業，道理如前卷54，1796頁所說可知。這是依作業等事來說明色聲香味觸五境的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">未六、依作業攝受辨4　申一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科依作業攝受辨，說明第六個因緣，依五根作業差別所攝受事，次第宣說十八界，分四科；第一科標，標出依五根作業差別攝受，宣說十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又由作業差別攝受故，次第宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又由五根作業差別所攝受事，而宣說十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4528"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">所以者何？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申三、釋5　酉一、眼界作業2　戌一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科眼界作業，說明眼界作業所攝事，又分二科；第一科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由眼能見種種諸色；往還無失；威儀不亂；記識他身曾見不見及怨親中；了悟方所，宣示於他，起想言說；覩眾舞樂角力戲等，廣受種種世間喜樂，長養依身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於眼睛能夠看到種種的色法；在道路來來往往時，不會走錯路；行住坐臥四威儀有條不紊；能夠認識他人的身相，知道是否看過這個人，是親家、怨家、或是非親非怨；了知處所的差別，告訴他人，令人生起名想而能言說；依眼觀看種種唱歌、跳舞、角力、戲劇等事；以上這些事都要依止眼根才能成辦，使眾生廣受種種世間喜樂長養色身。眾生日常生活中時時需要依眼做種種事，維持生命、滋潤生命、長養生命。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類，有無量種眼界作業。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，我們活在這個世間，如讀書、走路、煮飯、遊玩等有無量種事，都必須靠眼睛來完成，所以說有無量種眼界作業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉二、耳界作業2　戌一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科耳界作業，說明耳根作業所攝事，分二科；第一科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由耳能聞種種音聲，因此了悟善說、惡說種種義理，起諸言論；因聞種種微妙樂音，廣受種種世間喜樂，長養依身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　耳根必須以聲音為食。佛陀在《阿含經》說，眼睛以色為食物；耳根以聲音為食物，六根都要有食物滋養才能夠活得下去。我們欲界的人，由耳能夠聽種種的音聲，聽到聲音以後，就知道這是善說、惡說，是合理或是不合道理的，然後能夠發出種種的語言。此外耳根可受用種種好聽的音樂，所以世間人常開鋼琴演奏會、小提琴演奏會，或是交響樂表演。美妙的音樂，能攝益身心、令人心情愉快。由耳界的功能，廣受種種世間喜樂，長養色身，眾生用到耳根的地方也是蠻多的，僅次於眼根。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類耳界作業，比前狹劣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，用到耳根的作業情況，比前面的眼根的範圍窄一點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉三、鼻界作業2　戌一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科鼻界作業，說明鼻作業所攝事，分二科；第一科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4529"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">鼻界能齅種種諸香，尋香而往，受諸喜樂，長養依身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由鼻根能齅種種諸香氣，追逐薰香馥郁，吸取悅鼻的香氣，領受喜樂，長養色身。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類鼻界作業，方前狹劣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，依照鼻根所作事而言，比前面耳根又少一點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉四、舌界作業2　戌一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科舌界作業，說明舌界作業所攝事，分二科；第一科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">舌界能嘗種種諸味，受諸喜樂，長養依身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　舌根能夠品嘗各式各樣食物的味道，美食佳餚，如天甘露，不僅能維持生命，對治飢渴，使身體健康，還能令人身心愉悅，受諸喜樂，長養色身。我們吃東西是吃食物的香和味，不是吃色，也不能吃聲。嚐種種的味道，心情快樂，可以長養所依身，使身體增長壯大。像小孩子的成長，必須吃種種的食物；有些人心情不好就去吃東西，吃東西使他快樂，由此長養他的色身。但是舌根用的地方還是少，人不能整天都吃東西，肚子餓了才能吃。而眼睛好像很少有飽的時候，耳根也可以一直聽，好聽的音樂整天都聽也不礙事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類舌界作業，方前狹劣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，依照舌根所作事而言，比起用到鼻根的機會，舌根又用得少一點，範圍小一些。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">酉五、身界作業2　戌一、辨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科身界作業，說明身界作業所攝事，分二科；第一科辨，說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身界能觸種種所觸，受諸喜樂，雖能長養依身，然彼樂具，或於一時復為損害。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身根界能夠觸對種種柔軟細滑等觸，領受種種喜樂，雖能夠長養所依止的身體，然而使身體快樂的器具，有時候反而對身體有傷害。比如按摩器可以鬆弛肌肉，去除疲勞，可是一但漏電，可能生命難保。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戌二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是等類身界作業，最為狹劣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上所說，身體的作業是最少的，身界就是用來運動，通常早上運動一下，晚上運動一下。運用身根的機會比前面用舌根的機會又少一點。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4530"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">申四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">是名第六次第宣說因緣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這就是第六種因緣，約五根作業所攝事，而安立宣說十八界的次第。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》又由作業差別攝受故者：此中約彼眼等五根為論，說名次第，如文可知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是由眼耳鼻舌身五根為論，來說次第，如上文可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、總說意界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科總說意界，最後總說意界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於此眼等六種因緣差別中，意遍行故，最後宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼先說眼耳鼻舌身界？最後才說意界？在眼等六種因緣差別中，意遍於眼耳鼻舌身都有，所以最後才說意界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》意遍行故最後宣說者：謂如前說六種次第宣說因緣，不攝意界，由是遍行一切境故，是故最後別為宣說。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面所說的六種次第宣說因緣，都在形容用眼耳鼻舌身的情況，不包含意界，由於意遍於一切境界，有眼耳鼻舌身時，一定有意，故最後特別宣說意安立於五根之後。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、嗢柁南</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科嗢柁南，用一個偈頌歸納前文所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">為攝如是次第因緣，中嗢柁南曰：</span></strong></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眾多順世俗　喜樂與莊嚴　隨二種作業　故次第宣說</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為了攝受如是次第因緣，在文的中間用一個偈頌歸納前文所說。眾多是指眾多的因緣，六因緣中的第一個因緣依所行差別因緣；因為眼等所緣最多。順世俗是指第二個因緣，就是依世間俗事辨。喜樂指第三個因緣是依喜樂差別辨。與莊嚴，第四個因緣是依嚴飾差別辨。隨二種作業，第五及第六因緣是依作業等事辨、依作業攝受辨，這二種作業的情況，所以才次第宣說十八界為六根界、六塵界及六識界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、明所攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科明所攝，說明十八界能夠攝一切經中所說餘界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4531"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，此十八界，當知能攝一切經中所說餘界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，十八界能夠含攝一切經中所說的其他界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛在《雜阿含經》中常說到種種界，如《雜阿含經》卷16：有一次佛住王舍城迦蘭陀竹園。佛告諸比丘：「眾生常與界俱，與界和合。」什麼稱為與界俱？是指眾生不善心時與不善界俱，善心時與善界俱，鄙心時與鄙界俱，勝心時與勝界俱。這是要比丘們常與界俱，與界和合，應當善巧分別種種諸界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　界除了因義也有種類的意思，人們常說物以類聚，我們說法界、出家界、醫學界、科學界等世間有種種界。這種種界不超出十八界的根本範圍，都由十八界種子現前，產生無量有情差別。前面說，以十八界為基礎，有種種的界，非一界，依於十八界的現行，產生各式各樣的有情，他們有各式各樣的興格、作業等差別，這些界不離眼等五根、色等五塵及眼等五識和合運轉，交互作用而產生無量界。因此十八界，就能夠含攝一切經中所說的一切界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》能攝一切經中所說餘界者：如攝事分廣說諸界應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/96.htm#44564:72906">陵本九十六卷一頁7185</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　可以參考本論〈攝事分〉卷96，2821頁，該處詳細說明62界等種種界的建立差別，由彼處所說應能了知一切經中所說諸界的建立道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、釋妨難5　子一、色生鼻舌難2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋妨難，解釋他人提出的難問，分五科；第一科色生鼻舌難，說明色界為什麼會生出鼻根和舌根的難問，又分二科；第一科問，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：生色界者，已於境界而得離欲，何緣復生鼻、舌兩界？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：生到色界天的人，他們已經離欲界的欲，離欲才能夠得定，為什麼還生出鼻界和舌界？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、令端嚴</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科令端嚴，色界有情為身相端嚴，而有鼻界及舌界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：為令所依身端嚴故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：色界天人為了身相端嚴也有鼻界與舌界，這樣使他的身體看起來比較莊嚴。生到色界天的人，都是男眾，如果他們只有眼睛、耳朵，還有身體，沒有鼻子與嘴巴，想想看，好不好看？一定不好看，所以他們雖然沒有用鼻舌二識，還是有鼻舌二界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、未離欲</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科未離欲，說明色界中尚未離鼻舌二界的欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又色界中，於此二種未離欲故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又在色界中，還沒有離鼻根和舌根這二法的境界欲，因此還有鼻舌二界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》於此二種未離欲故者：謂生色界，雖於香、味境界而得離欲，然於一切色根未離欲故，是故復生鼻、舌兩界，由是說言二未離欲。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　生到色界的人，他們不用吃飯，雖然能夠離香界、味界這二種境界欲，可是他們尚未離一切色根的境界欲，因此又生鼻、舌兩界，所以說此二種未離欲故。為什麼色界天的人還有鼻界和舌界？第一種原因，是為了莊嚴，使令他的身體看起來比較好看。第二種，是對於這二法還沒有離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、尋伺有無難2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科尋伺有無難，尋就是粗的思惟觀察，伺就是細的思惟觀察，二禪以上就是無尋無伺地，分二科；第一科問，現在難問為什麼到二禪以上還有尋伺嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：生第二靜慮或生上地，若有尋有伺眼等識現在前，云何此地無尋無伺？若不現前，云何於彼有色諸根而能領受彼地境界？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：生到第二禪天，或生三禪、四禪的人，若是有尋有伺必須與眼等諸識同時現前活動，如果是這樣的話，怎麼可以說二禪以上稱為無尋無伺？若是尋伺不現前的話，為什麼二禪以上的人他們的有色諸根，能夠領受那一界地的境界？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　《八識規矩頌》說：「眼耳身三二地居」，初禪以下才有眼耳身三識，二禪以上全部都是意識相應，此處說若有尋有伺眼等識現在前，並不是說眼等識有尋伺。實際上前五識並不與尋伺相應，尋伺唯與意識相應，然而與五識同緣意識必與尋伺相應，所以文中如此難問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4532"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》有尋有伺眼等識現在前者：尋伺相應，唯意識有。今於此中，說眼等識隨意識轉，名眼等識有尋有伺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　尋伺唯與意識相應，現在此文意思是說，眼等識隨意識轉，稱為眼等識有尋有伺。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、答初問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科答初問，回答第一個問題。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：由有尋有伺諸識種子隨逐無尋無伺三摩地故，從彼起已，此得現前。又此起已，識現行時，復為無尋無伺三摩地種子之所隨逐，是故此地非是一向無尋無伺。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：由於和有尋有伺相應的意識種子，隨逐著二禪以上的無尋無伺定，從無尋無伺的三摩地出來以後，與尋伺相應的意識是可以現前的。又尋伺相應的分別意識生起來，與五識共緣境界時，還是有無尋無伺定的種子所隨逐。所以二禪以上無尋無伺定，不是一向完全無尋無伺，出定時也可以有尋有伺的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、答後問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答後問，回答後面的問題：為什麼〈無尋無伺地〉，他們的有色諸根能夠領受彼地境界？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由彼有情於諸尋伺以性離欲而離欲故，彼地雖名無尋無伺，此復現行，亦無過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於二禪以上的有情，心已離尋伺色聲香味觸的欲，二禪以上雖然是〈無尋無伺地〉，尋伺仍然可以現前；尋伺現前不是為了尋伺欲，而是依尋伺觀察境界，他的心已離欲，因此尋伺現行也沒有過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》以性離欲而離欲故等者：聲聞地說：若在定地，於緣最初率爾而起怱務行境，麤意言性，是名為尋。即於彼緣隨彼而起、隨彼而行徐歷行境，細意言性，是名為伺。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/33.htm#44580:27096">陵本三十三卷八頁2695</a>）由念正知能為對治，於自內體其心捨住，遠離尋伺塵濁法故，初靜慮地尋伺寂靜，不復現行，是名以性離欲而得離欲。有尋有伺地說：由離尋伺欲道理故，說名無尋無伺地，不由不現行故。乃至廣說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/04.htm#44580:2558">陵本四卷二頁265</a>）此中道理，準彼應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　〈聲聞地〉卷33說過什麼是尋？什麼是伺？若在定地，在所緣境上最初率爾而起的很匆忙的思惟觀察，這種行相較粗的第六意識，說名為尋；就在尋的所緣境上，隨尋而起，慢慢地觀察所緣境界，這種行相較細的第六意識，說名為伺。由於有正念正知，能夠對治欲的尋伺，在內心捨掉尋伺欲而住，遠離尋伺污濁的欲煩惱。入了二禪以後，初禪的欲尋伺已經寂靜，不會再現行。離欲界欲才能夠得到初禪，要得到二禪必須遠離初禪的欲尋伺。所以〈有尋有伺地〉卷4，110頁說：由遠離尋伺欲的道理，而安立〈無尋無伺地〉，並不是由於尋伺不現行，才是〈無尋無伺地〉。意思就是二禪還是有尋有伺，不過他這個尋伺是不和欲相應的，他沒有欲的尋伺，還可以起下地意識與眼耳身三識同取下地的境界。〈無尋無伺地〉的定義在於沒有尋伺欲，不在尋伺的現行與否，乃至還有一大段文，在此省略不說，這是卷4所說，此處道理，準照卷4所說可知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、眼等生二難</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科眼等生二難，解釋眼睛、耳朵、鼻子各有二分的難問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：何緣眼界、耳界、鼻界各生二分，非餘？答：為令依止得端嚴故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：為什麼我們的眼睛，耳朵、還有鼻孔都有兩個部分，但沒有兩個舌頭，也沒有兩個身體？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：為了使我們的身相能夠端正莊嚴。其他的論還多了一個理由，有兩個部分是為了識對境有比較明了的分別。為什麼要有兩個眼睛，是為使我們的眼識明了性比較強一點；二個眼在二邊，可以察覺到所見物的深度。二個耳朵在二邊，可以察覺聲音來自何方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4533"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、依生識難2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依生識難，依眼識、耳識、還有鼻識來難問，分二科；第一科問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：眼、耳與鼻諸識生時，為依二分，當言一耶？當言二耶？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：依眼、耳、鼻各有二個部分，生眼識、耳識和鼻識時，依止二個眼、耳、鼻應當說能生一個眼識、耳識和鼻識等識？還是各生出兩個眼識、耳識和鼻識等識？關於這個問題，詳細內容請參考引自福嚴佛學院的界處善巧之問答。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C56-01.htm">界處善巧之問答</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以及界處善巧之問答所連結檔</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　（連結：<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/C56-02.htm">二眼見色</a>）</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、標唯一</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科標唯一，標出唯一。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：當言唯一。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：應當說依止眼、耳、鼻各有二個部分都只能生出一個眼識、耳識、及鼻識。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋所以2　卯一、由識明了不明了生</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋所以，解釋道理，由於識依著其中的一分，分二科；第一科由識明了不明了生，有明了性或沒有明了性這一點來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？若彼一分無障不壞，識明了生；若彼有障，或復失壞，識不明了生故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　為什麼這樣說？因為如果其中有一個部分沒有障礙，沒有破壞，識可以很明了地現前；如果其中一分裡面有障礙，或是破壞了，識則不能很明了地現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、由識非色無方所別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由識非色無方所別，由於眼識、耳識、鼻識不是色法，沒有處所的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又識非色故，無有如色由方所別成二分義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又因為識不是色法，不會像色法一樣，在空間佔據處所，因此不像眼等佔據二邊的處所而分成二個部分。這段文是論主為簡別犢子部及上座部等執一眼見色的說法。據《阿毘達磨大毘婆沙論》卷13論主駁斥犢子部一眼見色之說時，說：若「一眼見色，非二眼」者，身諸分亦應不俱時覺觸！如身根兩臂相去雖遠，而得俱時覺觸生一身識；兩眼亦爾，相去雖遠，何妨俱時見色生一眼識？論中又說到不同部派提出四種疑慮，說明如下：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、總說四種疑慮</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　謂諸有情兩眼相去或半麻、一麻半，麥、一麥半，指、一指半，搩手 、一搩手半，弓、一弓半，俱盧舍 、一俱盧舍半，踰繕那、一踰繕那，或復乃至百踰繕那。如大海中有大身眾生，或長百踰（62a）繕那 ，乃至或長二千一百踰繕那；如曷邏呼 阿素洛王身量極大；又如天趣色究竟身，一萬六千踰繕那量──此等二眼相去甚遠，或有生疑「云何眼識依之而轉？」</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1.為「二眼識俱時各依一眼生」耶？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2.為「一眼識依一眼生已，復依第二眼轉」耶？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3.為「一眼識分為二分，於二眼處各半生」耶？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4.為「一眼識如橫一物通二眼」耶？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、別釋四種疑慮</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1.若「二眼識俱時各依一眼生」者，應一有情二心俱轉，此不應理。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2.若「一眼識依一眼生已，復依第二眼轉」者，則應一法二剎那住，然無是事。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3.若「一眼識分為二分，於二眼處各半生」者，則應一法體有二分，然一切法體無細分。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4.若「一眼識，如橫一物通二眼」者，則應一識亦是眼識亦是身識，二眼中間依身根故；然五識身所依各異、所緣各異，不應一識二依、二緣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　總之，欲令此疑得決定故，顯雖無有二眼識俱乃至無一識橫通二眼，然其非不依於二眼一眼識生，二眼雖隔百踰繕那，亦無有過。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文若依據安慧法師所作《大乘法苑義林章補闕》卷7有不同看法，論中提問：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三（眼耳鼻）各有二分，識依一生，為依二起？答：依一依二，理並無妨。閉一亦得，觀聞齅等開二識生，得明盛故。意指依一眼見色或二眼見色都可以，並且見聞嗅時許可二識得生，令所緣境得明盛故。不過本論指一二眼一眼識生，論點同於《大毗婆沙論》。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4534"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若彼一分無障不壞等者：此中無障，謂四種障所不障礙。一、覆蔽障，二、隱沒障，三、映奪障，四、幻惑障。又復不壞亦有二因。一、不滅壞故；二、不羸劣故。如意地說。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/03.htm#44594:1907">陵本三卷五頁206</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此處無障，是指沒有四種障礙的現前。四種障礙是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、覆蔽障：覆蓋遮住的障礙，比如眼睛要見色時，有黑布或其他物體覆蓋遮住就看不到了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、隱沒障：隱藏埋沒的障礙，比如眼睛看色塵時，用藥草或是神通的力量，使色法不見了，這是隱沒障。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、映奪障：映蔽侵奪的障礙，比如太陽一出來就映奪星星的光明，鑽石一出現就映奪珍珠的光彩。如要看一個東西，可是被其他更有強大吸引力的東西所映奪時，就看不到了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、幻惑障：幻化迷惑的障礙，比如變魔術，將手帕變成兔子，依幻術迷惑真相，使人誤以為是真的兔子，不知是手帕。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果沒有這些障礙時，眼識、或是耳識、或是鼻識，就能明了現前。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又不壞有二種原因：一、不滅壞故，沒有完全消滅破壞；二、不羸劣故，沒有羸弱下劣。比如眼睛瞎了稱作滅壞，就完全看不到。眼根若有近視或閃光，看東西就不準確而羸劣，反之眼睛沒有瞎也沒有其它毛病，識的明了性強，視力就很好。如〈本地分‧意地〉卷3，90頁所說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、因果俱有難2　丑一、問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科因果俱有難，分二科；第一科問，經部師難問，眼根和眼識如果是因果的關係，怎麼可以同時現前？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：眼與眼識若是因果，云何俱有？若俱有者，云何得成因果兩性？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：眼與眼識如果是因果關係，怎麼可以同時而有？如果同時而有，怎麼能說是因果？聲聞乘經部師認為前因後果，因果是不能同時的。大乘主張有二種因果，一種是同時因果，一種是異時因果。其中種子生現行，現行生種子，三法同時，是同時因果；造善惡因，得異熟果，那是異時因果。此處所說同時因果，眼識生必依眼根，它們同時存在，彼此的因果關係是約建立因即增上緣而說的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、答2　寅一、正顯2　卯一、舉眼與眼識3　辰一、標義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科答，回答，分二科；第一科正顯，正面地顯示，又分二科；第一科舉眼與眼識，舉出眼根和眼識的關係，又分三科；第一科標義，先標出道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">答：識依眼生，非如種芽因果道理。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：眼識依眼根而生，這不像種子生出芽的因果道理。種子要長出芽還要經過一段時間。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋由</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋由，解釋理由。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何以故？眼與眼識，非正生因，唯建立因。是故此二俱時而有，因果性成。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼說？眼根與眼識有因果關係，不是指正生因，正生因就是眼根為種子，生出眼識，才是正生因。現在是眼識以眼根為依止生出眼識，所以是唯建立因，也就是增上緣。此處是依增上緣來說他們二個同時而有，有因果性，不是依種子，不依因緣來說他們的因果性。所以眼根與眼識同時而有，而且具因果關係。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、引喻</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科引喻，舉出一個譬喻來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">猶如燈焰光明道理。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　眼根和眼識的因果關係，就好像燈焰會發出種種光明的道理一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例餘與諸識</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘與諸識，推例餘根與餘識的道理也一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼與眼識，耳、鼻、舌、身與彼諸識，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼根和眼識的因果關係是這樣的，耳鼻舌身與耳識、鼻識、舌識、身識也是同樣的道理，也是這樣說明就可以了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4535"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、反成</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科反成，接著反面來證成自己的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若異此者，雖有自種，無所依故，眼等諸識應不得生。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果不依增上緣來建立根識的因果關係的話，雖然眼等識也有種子，而且不會間斷，若沒有依止的根，眼等諸識是不能現前的，所以必須用增上緣來建立，因此說他們的因果關係是建立因，而不是正生因。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、辨彼轉3　子一、於欲界2　丑一、不決定轉2　寅一、舉眼界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科辨彼轉，說明生三界眼等諸界的有、無及定、不定的道理，分三科；第一科於欲界，說明欲界眼、耳、鼻、舌界及彼識界，又分二科；第一科不決定轉，說明眼、耳、鼻、舌界及彼識界不決定現行的情況，又分二科；第一科舉眼界，先舉出眼界為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若於欲界或生或長，當言眼界決定轉耶？答：此非一向。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果在欲界受生或是長大的人，應該說他眼界一定會現前嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：不一定會現前，也有人生來就盲的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、例餘界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘界，耳、鼻、舌界及彼識界如眼界不一定現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼界，耳、鼻、舌界及彼識界，當知亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如眼界不一定現前，耳界、鼻界、舌界，以及眼耳鼻舌識界也是一樣，不一定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、決定轉2　寅一、舉身界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科決定轉，身界決定現前，分二科；第一科舉身界，舉身界為例。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">身界決定轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　身界決定現前，一定要有身體。欲界的人，不一定有眼、耳、鼻、舌，但是一定會有身界的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、例餘界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例餘界，如身界，身識界，意界，法界，意識界，色、聲、香、味、觸界也決定現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是身識界，意界，法界，意識界，色、聲、香、味、觸界亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如身界決定現前，如是身識界、意界、意所取的法界、意識界，以及為欲界眾生所受用的色、聲、香、味、觸界也是一樣，一定決定現前的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、於色界3　丑一、舉眼界</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於色界，說明生色界的情況，分三科；第一科舉眼界，色界的人的眼界決定現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">問：若於色界或生或長，當言眼界決定轉耶？答：決定轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　問：如果生在色界天的人，或在那裡成長的人，他的眼界一定會現前嗎？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　答：他的眼界一定現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="56p4536"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》若於色界或生或長等者：此說色界眼決定轉，與有色界義有差別。有色界中，若眼未生，或生已失，或不得眼，如前已說，當知彼約欲界名有色界。今此不爾，唯說色界，不通餘界，由是故言眼決定轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　色界天人是化生的，他們決定會有眼界，這是與欲界不一樣的。欲界有情，從在羯羅藍位直到住胎位，那時還沒有到根位時，眼還沒有生出來；或生出眼根又失掉；或沒有眼根；如前文已說；應當知道前面說的有色界是指欲界。現在此處不是指欲界，而是指色界，不通餘界，因此說眼決定現前。色界天的人是化生，一定有眼根；但是欲界的人就不一定了。有時候一生出來就盲聾瘖啞，眼不能見、耳不能聽、口不能言都有可能，所以不一定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、例耳等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例耳等，耳等界也決定現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如眼界，如是耳、鼻、舌、身界，眼、耳、身識界亦爾。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如色界天人眼界一定現前，如是耳界、鼻界、舌界，眼識界、耳識界、身識界三個識界，也是一樣一定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、簡差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科簡差別，簡別色界沒有香界、味界、及鼻識界和舌識界。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">除香、味界及彼識界，餘一切界亦決定轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　除香界、味界、鼻識界及舌識界不會現前，因為色界天人沒有段食，沒有香界和味界，也沒有鼻識界和舌識界。除了這四界，十八界裡面的其他界也一定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》餘一切界亦決定轉者：謂色、聲、觸界，意界，法界，意識界，名餘一切應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　在十八界中，色界天人除了香界、味界、鼻識界及舌識界以外，所餘的色界、聲界、觸界，意界、法界、意識界，一定會現前的。色界天人有十四個界決定會現前。相對於欲界來說，欲界的十八界中，眼耳鼻舌，眼識、耳識、鼻識、舌識，有八個不一定會現前，決定會現前的就是身界、身識界，意界、法界、意識界，色聲香味觸法，欲界的人有十界決定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、於無色界2　丑一、簡差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科於無色界，說明無色界天諸界，分二科；第一科簡差別，先簡別與欲色界的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">於無色界或生或長，除意界、法界、意識界，餘定不轉，唯除自在所獲諸色。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　無色界天的人，除了意界、法界、意識界，這三界一定現前，其他的一定不會現前，因為他們沒有色法，少掉五根界、五塵界、五識界，只剩下意界、法界、意識界這三界。當然除外的就是定自在所生色也可現前，就另當別論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、顯定轉</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科顯定轉，在無色界中意界、法界、意識界，三界決定會現前。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">當知三界於彼定轉。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　應當了知意界、法界、意識界三界在無色界中決定會現前。</span></span></span></div>
